vedavedāṅgasaṃpanno brāhmaṇo vātra jāyate
punaḥ prāgvāsanāyogāddhārmiko vedapāragaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
trisaṃdhyam arcayed īśam agnikāryaṃ ca śaktitaḥ
śivasnānaṃ purā kṛtvā tattvaśuddhiṃ ca pūrvavat
puṣpahastaḥ praviśyātha pūjāsthānaṃ samāhitaḥ
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dāhanāplāvanāni ca
vijñānena tanuṃ kṛtvā brahmāgnerapi yatnataḥ
avyaktabuddhyahaṅkāratanmātrāsaṃbhavāṃ tanum
śivāmṛtena saṃpūtaṃ śivasya ca yathātatham
adhoniṣṭhyā vitastyāṃ tu nābhyāmupari tiṣṭhati
hṛdayaṃ tadvijānīyādviśvasyāyatanaṃ mahat
hṛtpadmakarṇikāyāṃ tu devaṃ sākṣātsadāśivam
pañcavaktraṃ daśabhujaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
prativaktraṃ trinetraṃ ca śaśāṅkakṛtaśekharam
ūrdhvaṃ vaktraṃ sitaṃ dhyāyetpūrvaṃ kuṅkumasannibham
nīlābhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ vaktramatiraktaṃ tathottaram
gokṣīradhavalaṃ divyaṃ paścimaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
śūlaṃ paraśukhaṅgaṃ ca vajraṃ śaktiṃ ca dakṣiṇe
vāme pāśāṅkuśaṃ ghaṇṭāṃ nāgaṃ nārācamuttamam
varadābhayahastaṃ vā śeṣaṃ pūrvavadeva tu
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ citrāṃbaradharaṃ śivam
uktāni pañca brahmāṇi śivāṅgāni śṛṇuṣva me
śaktibhūtāni ca tathā hṛdayādīni suvrata
oṃ īśānaḥ sarvavidyānāṃ hṛdayāya śaktibījāya namaḥ
oṃ īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāmamṛtāya śirasenamaḥ
oṃ brahmādhipataye kālāgnirupāya śikhāyai namaḥ
oṃ brahmaṇodhipataye kālacaṇḍamārutāya kavacāya namaḥ
oṃ brahmaṇe bṛṃhaṇāya jñānamūrtaye netrāya namaḥ
oṃ śivāya sadāśivāya pāśupatāsrāya apratihatāya phaṭphaṭ
oṃ haṃsaśikhāya vidyādehāya ātmasvarūpāya parāparāya śivāya śivatamāya namaḥ
kathitāni śivāṅgāni mūrtividyā ca tasya vai
brahmāṅgamūrti vidyāṅgasahitāṃ śivaśāsane
saurāṇi ca pravakṣyāmi bāṣkalādyāni suvrata
aṅgāni sarvavedeṣu sārabhūtāni suvrata
oṃbhūḥ oṃbhuvaḥ oṃ svaḥ oṃmahaḥ oñjanaḥ ontapaḥ oṃsatyam oṃṛtam oṃbrahmānavākṣaramayaṃ mantraṃ bāṣkalaṃ parikīrtitam
namaḥ sūryāya khakholkāya namaḥ
navākṣareṇa dīptādya mūlamantreṇa bhāskaram
pūjayedaṅgamantrāṇi kathayāmi samāsataḥ
oṃbhūḥ brahmaṇe hṛdayāya namaḥ
oṃbhuvaḥ viṣṇave śirase namaḥ
oṃsvaḥ rudrāya śikhāyai namaḥ oṃbhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ jvālāmāninyai devāya namaḥ oṃmahaḥ maheśvarāya kavacāya namaḥ
oñjanaḥ śivāya netrebhyo namaḥ
evaṃ prasaṃgādeveha saurāṇi kathitāni ha
itthaṃ mantramayaṃ devaṃ pūjayeddhṛdayāṃbuje
manasā sarvakāryāṇi śivāgnau devamīśvaram
pañcabrahmāṅgasaṃbhūtaṃ śivamūrtiṃ sadāśivam
raktapadmāsanāsīnaṃ sakalīkṛtya yatnataḥ
mūlena mūrtimantreṇa brahmāṅgādyaistū suvrata
samidājyāhutīrhutvā manasā candramaṇḍalāt
candrasthānātsamutpannāṃ pūrṇadhārāmanusmaret
pūrṇāhutividhānena jñānināṃ śivaśāsane
śivaṃ vaktragataṃ dhyāyettejomātraṃ ca śāṅkaram
lalāṭe devadeveśaṃ bhramadhye vā smaretpunaḥ
śuddhadīpaśikhākāraṃ bhāvayedbhavanāśanam
liṅge ca pūjayeddevaṃ sthaṇḍile vā sadāśivam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge trayoviṃśatitamodhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
vyākhyāṃ pūjāvidānasya pravadāmi samāsataḥ
śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa śivena kathitaṃ purā
athobhau candanacarcitau hastau vauṣaḍantenādyañjaliṃ kṛtvā mūrtividyāśivādīni japtvā aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhikānta īśānādyaṃ kaniṣṭhikādimadhyamāntaṃ hṛdayāditṛtīyāntaṃ turīyamaṅguṣṭhenānāmikayā pañcamaṃ taladvayena ṣaṣṭhaṃ tarjanyaṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ nārācastraprayogeṇa punarapi mūlaṃ japtvā turīyenāvaguṇṭhya śivahastamityucyate
śivārcaṃnā tena hastena kāryā
kṣmāmbhognivāyuvyomāntaṃ pañcacatuḥśuddhakoṭyante dhārāsahitena vyavasthāpya tattśuddhiṃ pūrvaṃ kuryāt
tattvaśuddhiḥ ṣaṣṭhena sadyena tṛtīyena phaḍantāddharāśuddhiḥ
ṣaṣṭhasahitena sadyena tṛtīyena phaḍantena vāritattvaśuddhiḥ
vāhneyatṛtīyena phaṇḍatenāgniśuddhiḥ
vāyavyacaturthena ṣaṣṭhasahitena phaḍantena vāyuśuddhiḥ
ṣaṣṭhena sasadyena tṛtīyena phaḍantenākāśaśuddhiḥ
upasaṃhṛtyaivaṃ sadyaṣaṣṭhena tṛtīyena mūlena phaḍantena tāḍanaṃ tṛtīyena saṃpuṭīkṛtyagrahaṇaṃ mūlameva yonibījena saṃpuṭīkṛtvā bandhanaṃ bandhaḥ
evaṃ kṣāntātītādinivṛttiparyantaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā praṇavena tattvatrayakamanudhyāya ātmānaṃ dīpaśikhākāraṃ puryaṣṭakasahitaṃ trayātītaṃ śaktikṣobheṇāmṛtadhārāṃ suṣumṇāyāṃ dhyātvā
śāntyatītādinivṛttiparyantānāṃ cāntarnādabindvakārokāramakārāntaṃ śivaṃ sadāśivaṃ rudraviṣṇubrahmāntaṃ sṛṣṭimeṇāmṛtīkaraṇaṃ brahmanyāsaṃ kṛtvā pañcavaktreṣu pañcadaśanayanaṃ vinyasya mūlena pādādikeśāntaṃ mahāmudrāmapi baddhvā śivohamiti dhyātvā śaktyādīni vinyasyahṛdi śaktyābījāṅkurānantarātsasuṣirasūtrakaṇṭakapatrakesaradharmajñānavairāgyaiśvaryasūryasomāgnivāmājyeṣṭhāraudrīkālīkalavikaraṇībalavikaraṇībala prathamanīsarvabhūtadamanīḥ kesareṣu karṇikāyāṃ manonmanīmapi dhyātvā
āsanaṃ parikalpyaivaṃ sarvopacārasahitaṃ bahiryogopacāreṇāntaḥkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā nābhau vahnikuṇḍe pūrvavadāsanaṃ parikalpya sadāśivaṃ dhyātvā binduto 'mṛtadhārāṃ śivamaṇḍale nipatitāṃ dhyātvā lalāṭe maheśvaraṃ dīpaśikhākāraṃ dhyātvā ātmaśuddhiritthaṃ prāṇāpānau saṃyamya suṣumṇayā vāyuṃ vyavasthāpya ṣaṣṭhena tālumudrāṃ kṛtvā digbandhaṃ kṛtvā ṣaṣṭhena sthānaśuddhirvastrādi pūtāntararghyapātrādiṣu praṇavena tattvatrayaṃ vinyasya tadupari bunduṃ dhyātvā vipūrya dravyāṇi ca vidhāya amṛtaplāvanaṃ kṛtvā pādyapātrādiṣu teṣāmarghyavadāsanaṃ parikalpya saṃhitayābhimantryādyenābhyarcya dvitīyenāmṛtīkṛtvā tṛtīyena viśodhyacaturthenāvaguṇṭhya pañcamonāvalokyaṣaṣṭhena rakṣāṃvidhāya caturthena kuśapuñjenārghyāṃbhasābhyukṣya ātmānamapi dravyāṇi punarghyāṃbhasābyukṣya sapuṣpeṇa sarvadravyāṇi pṛthakpṛthak śodhayet
aghoreṇa ābharaṇaṃ puruṣeṇa naivedyam
īśānena puṣpāṇi athābhimantrayet
śivagāyatryā śeṣaṃ prokṣayet
pañcāmṛtapañcagavyādīni brahmāṅgamūlādyairābhimantrayet
pṛthakpṛthaṅmūlenārghyaṃ dhūpaṃ dattvācamanīyaṃ ca teṣāmapi dhenumudrā ca darśayitvā kavacenāvaguṇṭhyāstreṇa rakṣāṃ ca vidhāya dravyaśuddhiṃ kuryāt
arghyodakamagre hṛdā gandhamādāyāstreṇa viśodhya pūjāprabhṛtikaraṇaṃ rakṣāntaṃ kṛtvaivaṃ dravyaśuddhiṃ pūjāsamarpaṇāntaṃ maunamāsthāya puṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā sarvamantrāṇi praṇavādinamontājjapitvā puṣpāñjaliṃ tyajenmantraśuddhirittham
agre sāmānyārghyapātraṃ payasāpūrya gandhapuṣpādinā saṃhitayābhimantrya dhenamudrāṃ dattvā kavacenāvaguṇṭhyāstreṇa rakṣayet
pūjāṃ paryuṣitāṃ gāyatryā samabhyarcya sāmānyārghyaṃ dattvā gandhapuṣpadhūpācamanīyaṃ svadhāntaṃ namontaṃ vā datvā brahmabhiḥ pṛthakpṛthakpuṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā phaḍantāstreṇa nirmalyaṃ vyapohya īśānyāṃ caṇḍamabhyarcyāsanamūrti caṇḍaṃ sāmānyāstreṇa liṅgapīṭhaṃ śivaṃ pāśupatāstreṇa viśodhya mūrdhni puṣpaṃ nidhāya pūjayelliṅgaśuddhiḥ
āsanaṃ kūrmaśilāyāṃ bījāṅkuraṃ tadupari brahmaśilāyāmanantanālasuṣire sūtrapatrakaṇṭakakarṇikākesaradharmajñānavairāgyaiśvaryasūryasomāgnikesaraśaktiṃ manonmanīṃ karṇikāyāṃ manonmanenānantāsanāyeti samāsenāsanaṃ parikalpya tadupari nivṛttyādikalāmayaṃ ṣaṅvidhasahitaṃ karmakalāṅgadehaṃ sadāśivaṃ bhāvayet
ubhābhyāṃ sapuṣpābhyāṃ hastābhyāmaṅguṣṭhena puṣpamāpīḍya āpāhanamudrayā śanaiḥśanaiḥ hṛdayādimastamāropya hṛdā saha mūlaṃ plutamuccāryasadyena bindusthānādabhyadhikaṃ dīpaśikhākāraṃ sarvatomukhahastaṃ vyāpyavyāpakamābāhya sthāpayet
pūrvahṛdā śivaśaktisamavāyena paramīkaraṇamamṛtīkaraṇaṃ hṛdayādimūlena sadyenāvāhanaṃ hṛdā mūlopari aghoreṇa sannirodaṃ hṛdā mūlopari puruṣeṇa sānnidhyaṃ hṛdā mūlena īśānena pūjayediti upadeśaḥ
rūpakadhyānaṃ kṛtvā mūlena namaskārāntamāpādya svadhāntamācamanīyaṃ sarvaṃ namaskārāntaṃ vā svāhākārāntamarghyaṃ mūlena puṣpāñjaliṃ vauṣaḍantena sarvaṃ namaskārāntaṃ hṛdā vā īśānena vā rudragāyatryā oṃnamaḥ śivāyeti mūlamantreṇa vā pūjayet
puṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā punardhūṣācamanīyaṃ ṣaṣṭhena puṣpāvasaraṇaṃ visarjanaṃ mantrodakena mūlena saṃsnāpya sarvadravyābhiṣekamīśānena pratidravyamaṣṭapuṣpaṃ dattvaivamarghyaṃ ca gandhapuṣpadhūpācamanīyaṃ phaḍantāstreṇa pūjāpasaraṇaṃ śuddhodakena mūlena saṃsnāpya piṣṭāmalagādibhiḥ
uṣṇodakena haridrādyena liṅgamūrti pīṭhasahitāṃ viśodhya gandhodakahiraṇyodakamantrodakena rudrādhyāyaṃ paṭhamānaḥ nīlarudratvaritarudrapañcabrahmādibhiḥ namaḥ śivāyeti snāpayet
mūrdhni puṣpaṃ nidhāyaivaṃ na śūnyaṃ liṅgamastakaṃ kuryādatra ślokaḥ
yasya rāṣṭre tu liṅgasya mastakaṃ śūnyalakṣaṇam
tasyālakṣmīrmahā rogo durbhikṣaṃ vāhanakṣayaḥ
śūnye liṅge svayaṃ rājā rāṣṭraṃ caiva praṇaśyati
evaṃ susnāpyārghyañca dattvā saṃmṛjya vastreṇa gandhapuṣpavastrālaṅkārādīṃśca mūlena dadyāt
dhūpācamanīyadīpanaivedyādīṃśca mūlena pradhānenopari pūjanaṃ pavitrīkaraṇamityuktam
ārārtidīpādīṃścaiva dhenumudrāmudritāni kavacenāvaguṇṭhināni ṣaṣṭhena rakṣitāni liṅge ca liṅgasyādhaḥ sādhāraṇaṃ ca darśayet
sakaladhyānaṃ niṣkalasmāraṇaṃ parāvaradhyānaṃ mūlamantrajapaḥ
daśāṃśaṃ brahmāṅgajapasamarpaṇamātmanivedanastutinamaskārādayaśca gurupūjā ca pūrvano dakṣiṇe vināyakasya
ādau cānte ca saṃpūjyo vighneśo jagadīśvaraḥ
yaḥ śivaṃ pūjayedevaṃ liṅge vā sthāṇḍilepi vā
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ varṣamātreṇa karmaṇā
liṅgārcakaśca ṣaṇmāsānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā
sapta pradakṣiṇāḥ kṛtvā daṇḍavatpraṇamedvudhaḥ
bhogārthī bhogamāpnoti rājyārthī rājyamāpnuyāt
putrārthī tanayaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rogī rogātpramucyate
yānyāṃścintayate kāmāṃstāṃnprāpnoti mānavaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge caturviśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
śivāgnikāryaṃ vakṣyāmi śivena paribhāṣitam
janayitvāgrataḥ prācīṃ śubhe deśe susaṃskṛte
pūrvāgramuttarāgraṃ ca kuryātsūtratrayaṃśubham
caturastrīkṛte kṣetre kuryātkuṇḍāni yatnataḥ
catustridvyaṅgulāyāmā mekhalā hastamātrataḥ
hastamātraṃ bhavetkuṇḍaṃ yoniḥ prādeśamātrataḥ
kuṇḍamadhye tu nābhiḥ syādaṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam
prādeśamātraṃ vidhinā kārayedbrahmaṇaḥ suta
ṣaṣṭhenollekhanaṃ proktaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ varmaṇā smṛtam
netreṇālokya vai kuṇḍaṃ ṣaḍrekhāḥ kārayedbudhaḥ
prāgāyatena viprendra brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
uttarāgrāḥ śivā rekhāḥ prokṣayedvarmaṇā punaḥ
śamīpippalasaṃbhūtāmaraṇīṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulām
mathitvā vahnibījena śaktinyāsaṃ hṛdaiva tu
tūṣṇīṃ prādeśamātraistu yājñikaiḥ śakalaiḥ śubhaiḥ
parisaṃmohanaṃ kuryājjalenāṣṭasu dikṣu vai
uttarāgraṃ purastāddhi prāgagraṃ dakṣiṇe punaḥ
saumyasyoparicāndrāgnaṃ vāruṇāgnamadhastataḥ
dvandvarūpeṇa pātrāṇi barhaḥṣvāsādya suvrata
pūjayenmūlamantreṇa paścāddhomaṃ samācaret
prokṣaṇīpātramādāya pūrayedaṃbunā punaḥ
plāvayecca kuśāgraṃ tu vasoḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ
vikīrya sarvapātrāṇi susaṃprokṣya vidhānataḥ
praṇītāpātramādāya pūrayedaṃbunā punaḥ
hastābhyāṃ nāsikaṃ pātramaiśānyāṃ diśi vinyaset
ājyādhiśrayaṇaṃ kuryātpaścimottarataḥ śubham
bhasmamiśrāṃstathāṅgārān grāhayetsakalena vai
paścimottarato nītvā tatra cājyaṃ pratāpayet
tānsarvāṃstatra niḥkṣipya cāgre cājyaṃ nidhāpayet
aṅguṣṭhamātrau tu kuśau prakṣālya vidhinaiva tu
athāpakarṣayet pātraṃ krameṇottarapaścime
saṃyujya cāgniṃ kāṣṭhena prakṣālyāropya paścime
pṛthagādāya hastābhyāṃ pravāheṇa yathākramam
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu ubhābhyāṃ mūlavidyayā
rājataṃ vā yathānyāyaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
athavā yājñikairvṛkṣaiḥ kartavyau sruksruvā vubhau
ṣaḍaṅgulaparīṇāhṝṃ daṇḍamūlaṃ mahāmune
tadardhaṃ kaṇṭhānālaṃ syātpuṣkaraṃ mūlavadbhavet
govālasadṛśaṃ daṇḍaṃ mruvāgraṃ nāsikāsamam
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulāyāmamaṣṭāṅgulasavistaram
saptāṅgulaṃ bhavedāsyaṃ vistarāyāmataḥ punaḥ
tribhāgaikaṃ bhavedagraṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ parityajet
kaṇṭhaṃ ca dvyaṅgulāyāmaṃ vistāraṃ caturaṅgulam
vediraṣṭāṅgulāyāmāvistārastatpramāṇataḥ
bilaṃ suvartitaṃ kuryādaṣṭapatraṃ sukarṇikam
parito bilabāhye tu paṭṭikārdhāṅgulena tu
yavadvayapramāṇena tadbrāhme paṭṭikā bhavet
vedikāmadhyato randhraṃ kaniṣṭhāṅgulamānataḥ
khātaṃ yāvanmukhāntaḥ syādbilamānaṃ tu nimragam
daṇḍaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ nālaṃ daṇḍāgre daṇḍikātrayam
trayodaśāṅgulāyāmaṃ daṇḍamūle ghaṭaṃ bhavet
dvyaṅgulastu bhavetkuṃbho nābhiṃ vidyāddaśāṅgulam
vedimadhye tathā kṛtvā pādaṃ kuryācca dvyaṅgulam
padmapṛṣṭhasamākāraṃ pādaṃ vai karṇikākṛtim
gajoṣṭhasadṛśākāraṃ tasya pṛṣṭhākṛtirbhavet
abhicārādikāryeṣu kuryātkṛṣṇāyasena tu
mūlaṃ mūlena vidhinā agnau tāpya hṛdā punaḥ
ājyasthālī praṇītā ca prokṣaṇī tisra eva ca
sauvarṇī rājatī vāpi tāmrī vā mṛnmayī tu vā
anyathā naiva kartavyaṃ śāntike pauṣṭike śubhe
āyasī tvabhicāre tu śāntike mṛnmayī tu vā
ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ suvistīrṇaṃ pātrāṇāṃ mukhamucyate
prokṣaṇī dvyaṅgulotsedhā praṇītā dvyaṅgulādhikā
ājyasthālī tatastasyā utsedho dvyaṅgulādhikaḥ
madhyāṅgulaparīṇāhā avakraā nirvraṇāḥ samāḥ
dvātriṃśadaṅgulāyāmāstisraḥ paridhayaḥsmṛtāḥ
dvātriṃśadaṅgulāyāmaistriṃśaddarbhaiḥ paristaret
abhicārādikāryeṣu śivāgnyādhānavarjitam
akomalāḥ sthirā vipra saṃgrāhyastvābhicārike
samagrāḥ susamāḥ sthūlāḥ kaniṣṭhāṅgulasaṃmitāḥ
avakraānirvraṇāḥ srigdhā dvādaśāṅgulasaṃmitāḥ
gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ tataḥ śreṣṭha kāpilaṃ tu tato 'dhikam
āhutīnāṃ gramaṇaṃ tu mruvaṃ pūrṇaṃ yathā bhavet
annamakṣapramāṇaṃ syācchuktimātreṇa vai tilaḥ
yavānāṃ ca tadardhaṃ syātphalānāṃ svapramāṇataḥ
catuḥmruvapramāṇena mrucā pūrṇāhutirbhavet
tadardhaṃ sviṣṭakṛtproktaṃ śeṣaṃ sarvamathāpi vā
śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ caiva śivāgnau juhuyātsadā
laukikāgnau mahābhāga mohanoccāṭanādayaḥ
śivāgniṃ janayitvā tu sarvakarmāṇe suvrata
athavā sarvakāryāṇi jihvāmātreṇa sidhyati
śivāgniriti viprendrā jihvāmātreṇa sādhakaḥ
oṃ bahurūpāyai madhyajihvāyai anekavarṇāyai dakṣiṇottaramadhyagāyai śāntipauṣṭikamokṣādiphalapradāyai svāhā
oṃ hiraṇyāyai cāmīkarābhāyai īśānajihvāyai jñānapradāyai svāhā
oṃ raktāyai raktavarṇāyai āgneyajihvāyai anekavarṇāyai vidveṣaṇamohanāyai svāhā
oṃ kṛṣṇāyai nairṛtajihvāyai māraṇāyai svāhā
oṃ suprabhāyaipaścimajihvāyai muktāphalāyai śāntikāyai pauṣṭikāyai svāhā
oṃ abhivyaktāyai vāyavyajihvāyai śatrūccāṭanāyai svāhā
naimittike ca vidhinā śivāgniṃ kārayetpunaḥ
nirīkṣaṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhena phaḍantena abhyukṣaṇaṃ caturthena khananotkiraṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhena pūraṇaṃ samīkaraṇamādyena secanaṃ vauṣaḍantena kṛṭṭanaṃ ṣaṣṭhena saṃmārjanopalepane turīyeṇa kuṇḍaparikalpanaṃ nivṛttyā tribhireva kuṇḍaparidhānaṃ caturthena kuṇḍārcanamādyena rekhācatuṣṭayasapādanaṃ ṣaṣṭhena phaḍantena vajrīkaraṇaṃ catuṣpadāpādanamādyena evaṃ kuṇḍasaṃskāramaṣṭādaśavidham
kuṇḍasaṃskārānantaramakṣapāṭanaṃ ṣaṣṭhena viṣṭaranyāsamādyena vajrāsane vāgīśvaryāvāhanam
oṃ hrīṃ vāgīśvarīṃ śyāmavarṇāṃ viśālākṣīṃ yauvanonmattavigrahām
ṛtumatīṃ vāgīśvaraśaktimāvāhayāmi
vāgīśvarīṃ pūjayāmi
roṃ iṃ vāgīśvarāya namaḥ
āvāhanasthāpanasannidhānasannirodhapūjāntaṃ vāgīśvarīṃ saṃbhāvya garbhādhānavahnisaṃskāram
ekavaktraṃ caturbhujaṃ śuddhasphaṭikābhaṃ varadābhayahastaṃ paraśumṛgadharaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitamāvāhayāmi
roṃ iṃ vāgīśvarāya namaḥ
āvāhanasthāpanasannidhānasannirodhapūjāntaṃ vāgīśvarīṃ saṃbhāvya garbhādhānavahnisaṃskāram
araṇījanitaṃ kāntodbhavaṃvā agnihotrajaṃvā tāmrapātreśarāvevā ānīya nirīkṣaṇatāḍanābhyukṣaṇaprakṣālanamādyenakravyādāśivaparityāgopi prathamena vahnestraikāraṇaṃ jaṭharabhrūmadyādāvāhyagniṃ vaikāraṇamūrtāvāgneyena uddīpanamādyena puraṣeṇa saṃhitayā dhāraṇā dhenumudrāṃ turīyeṇāvaguṇṭhya jānubhyāmavaniṃ gatvā śarāvotthāpanaṃ kuṇḍopari nidhāya pradakṣiṇamāvartya turīyeṇātmasammukhāṃ vāgīśvarīṃ garbhanāḍyāṃ garbhādhānāntarīyeṇa kamalapradānamādyena vauṣaḍantena kuśārghyaṃ dattvā indhanapradānamādyena prajvālanaṃ garbhādhānaṃ casadyenādyena pūjanaṃ vāmena pūjanaṃ dvitīyena sīmantonnayanamaghoreṇatṛtīyena pūjanam
avayavavyāptiktrodanaṃ vaktraniṣkṛtiriti tṛtīyena garbhajātakarmapuruṣeṇa pūjanaṃ turīyema ṣaṣṭhena prokṣaṇaṃ sūtakaśuddhaye cāgnisūnurakṣākusāstreṇa vaktreṇāgnau mūlamīsāgraṃ nairṛtimūlaṃ vāyavyāgraṃ vāyavyamūlamīśāgramiti kuśāstaramamitipūrvoktamidhmamagramūlaghṛtāktaṃ lālāpanodāya ṣaṣṭhena juhuyāt
pañcapūrvātikrameṇa paridhiviṣṭaranyāso 'pi ādyena viṣṭaropari hiraṇyagarbhaharanārāyaṇānapi pūjayet
indrādilokapālāṃśca pūjayet
vāgīśvaravāgīśvarīpūjādyenamudvāsya hutaṃ visarjayet
sraksruvasaṃskāramatho nirīkṣaṇaprokṣamatāḍanābhyukṣaṇādīni pūrvavat srak sruvaṃ ca hastadvaye gṛhītvā saṃsthāpanamādyena tāḍanamapi sruksruvopari darbhānulekhanamūlamadyamāgreṇa tritvena srakśākti sruvamapi śaṃbhuṃ dakṣiṇapārśve kuśopari śaktaye namaḥ śaṃbhave namaḥ
dhenumudrāṃ darśāyitvā turīyeṇāvaguṇṭhya ṣaṣṭhena rakṣāṃ vidhāya sruksruvasaṃskāraḥ pūrvamevoktaḥ
punarājyasaṃskāraḥ pūrvemevoktaḥ nirīkṣaṇaprokṣaṇatāḍanābhukṣaṇādīni pūrvavat
ājyapratāpanamaiśānyāṃ vā ṣaṣṭhena vedyupari vinyasya ghṛtapātraṃ vitastimātraṃ kuśapavitraṃ vāmahastāṅguṣṭhānāmikāgraṃ gṛhītvā dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhānāmikāmūlaṃ gṛhītvāgnijvālotpavanaṃ svāhāntena turīyeṇa punaḥ ṣaḍ darbhān gṛhītvā pūrvavatsvātmasaṃplavanaṃ svahāntenādyena kuśadvayapavitrabandhanaṃ cādyenaghṛte nyasediti pavitrīkaraṇam
saṃprokṣyāgnau nidhāpayediti nīrājanam
punardarbhān gṛhītvā kīṭakādi nirīkṣyārghyeṇa saṃprokṣya darbhānagnau nidhāya ityavadyotanam
darbhadvayaṃ gṛhītvāgnijvālayā ghṛtaṃ nirīkṣayet
darbheṇa gṛhītvā tenāgradvayena śuklapakṣadvayenādyeneti kṛṣṇapakṣasaṃpātanaṃ ghṛtaṃ tribhāgena vibhajya sruveṇaikabhāgenājyenāgnayesvāhā dvitīyenājyena somāya svāhā ājyena oṃ agnīṣomābhyāṃ svāhā ājyenāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā
punaḥ kuśena gṛhītvā saṃhitābhimantreṇa namontenābhimantrayet
abhimantrya denumudrāpradarśanakavacāvaguṇṭhanāstreṇa rakṣām
atha saṃskṛte nidhāpayet ājyasaṃskāraḥ
ājyena mrugvadanena cakraābhighāraṇaṃ śaktibījādiśānamūrtaye svāhā
pūrvavatpuruṣavattrāya svāhā aghorahṛdayāyasvāhā vāmadevāya guhyāya svāhā sadyojātamūrtaye svāhā
īśānamūrtaye tatpuruṣavaktrāya svāhā tatpuruṣavaktrāya aghorahṛdayāya svāhā aghorahṛdayāya vāmaguhyāya sadyojatamūrtaye svāhā iti vaktrasaṃdhānam
īśānamūrtaye tatpuruṣāya vaktrāya aghorahṛdayāya vāmadevāya guhyā sadyojātāya svāhā iti vaktrasaṃdhānam
īśānamūrtaye tatpuruṣāya vaktrāya aghorahṛdayāya vāmadevāya guhyāya sadyojātamūrtaye svāhā iti vaktraikyakaraṇam
śivāgniṃ janayitvaivaṃ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
kevalaṃ jihvayā vāpi śāntikādyāni sarvadā
daśa āhutāyo deyā yonibījena pañcadhā
āvāhanaṃ tathā nyāsaṃ yathā deve tathārcanam
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā sagarbhaṃ sarvasaṃmatam
āghārāvapi cādhāya cājyenaiva tu ṣaṇmuke
cakṣuṣī cājyabhāgau tu cāgnaye ca tathottare
akṣi vai dakṣiṇaṃ caiva cottaraṃ cottaraṃ tathā
dakṣiṇaṃ tu mahābhāga bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato dadyānmūlamantreṇa suvrata
sarvāvaraṇadevānāṃ pañcapañcaiva pūrvavat
īśānādikrameṇaiva śaktibījakrameṇa ca
prāyāścittamagoreṇa sveṣṭāntaṃ pūrvavatsmṛtam
ahiṃsakaṃ careddhomaṃ sādhako muktikāṅkṣakaḥ
dehasthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ śivaṃ sarvajagatpatim
taṃ jñātvā homayedbhaktyā prāṇāyāmena nityaśaḥ
bāhyahomapradātā tu pāṣāṇe darduro bhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
athavā devamīśānaṃ liṅge saṃpūjayecchivam
brāhmaṇaḥ śivabhaktaśca śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
ācāmedbrahmatīrthena brahmasūtrī hyudaṅmukhaḥ
athoṃnamaḥ śivāyeti tanuṃ kṛtvātmanaḥ punaḥ
sarvasmādadhikā pūjā aghoreśasya śūlinaḥ
sāmānyaṃ yajanaṃ sarvamagnikāryaṃ ca suvrata
aghorebhyaḥ praśāntahṛdayāya namaḥ
ghoraghoratarebhyaḥ jvālāmālinī śikāyai vaṣaṭ
sahasrākṣāya durbhedāya pāśupatāstrāya huṃ phaṭ
snātvācāmya tanuṃ kṛtvā samabhyukṣyāgamarṣaṇam
tarpaṇaṃ vidhinā cārghyaṃ bhānave bhānupūjanam
samaṃ cāghorapūjāyāṃ mantramātreṇa bheditam
mārgaśuddhistathā dvāri pūjāṃ vāstvadhipasya ca
kṛtvā karaṃ viśodhyāgre sa śubhāsanamāsthitaḥ
nāsāgrakamale sthāpya dagdhākṣaḥ kṣubhikāgninā
vāyunā prerya tadbhasma viśodhya ca śubhāṃ bhasā
aghoraṃ pañcadhā kṛtvā pañcāṅgasahitaṃ punaḥ
itthaṃ jñānākriyāmevaṃ vinyasya ca vidhānataḥ
nyāsāstrinetrasahito hṛdi dhyātvā varāsane
sāṃtyā bījāṅkurānantadharmādyairapi saṃyute
vāmādibhiśca sahite manonmanyāpyadhiṣṭhite
śivāsanetmamūrtisthamakṣayākāra rūpiṇam
aṣṭatriṃśatkalādehṝṃ tritattvasahitaṃ śivam
aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ devaṃ gajacarmottarīyakam
siṃhājināṃbaradharamaghoraṃ parameśvaram
dvātriṃśākṣararūpeṇa dvātriṃśacchaktibhirvṛtam
kapālamālābharaṇaṃ sarvavṛścikabhūthamaṇ
candrarekhādharaṃ śaktyā sahitaṃ nīlarūpiṇam
haste khaḍgaṃ kheṭakaṃ pāśamekeratnaiścitraṃ cāṅkuśaṃ nāgakakṣām
śarasanaṃ pāśupataṃ tathāstraṃ daṇḍaṃ ca khaṭvāṅgamathāpare ca
tantrīṃ ca ghaṇṭāṃ vipulaṃ ca śūlaṃ tathāpare ḍāmarukaṃ ca divyam
vajraṃ gadāṃ ṭaṅkamekaṃ ca dīptaṃ samudraraṃ hastamathāsya śaṃbhoḥ
aṣṭapuṣpādi gandhādi pūjāstutinivedanam
antarbaliṃ ca kuṇḍasya vāhneyena vidhānataḥ
maṇḍalaṃ vidhinā kṛtvā mantrairetairyathākramam
arghyaṃ gandhaṃ ca puṣpaṃ ca dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ ca suvratāḥ
vijñāpyaivaṃ visṛjyātha aṣṭapuṣpaiśca pūjanam
sarvasāmānyametaddhi pūjāyāṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktamaghorārcādi suvrata
aghorārcāvidhānaṃ ca liṅgevā sthāṇḍile 'pi vā
sthaṇḍilātkoṭiguṇitaṃ liṅgārcanamanuttamam
liṅgārcanarato vipro mahāpātakasaṃbhavaiḥ
liṅgasya darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ darśanātsparśanaṃ varam
arcanādadhikaṃ nāsti brahmaputra na saṃśayaḥ
varṣakoṭiśatenāpi vistareṇa na śakyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
śrutibhiḥ saṃmitaṃ sarvaṃ romaharṣaṇa suvrata
jayābhiṣeka īśena kathito manave purā
hitāya meruśikhare kṣatriyāṇāṃ triśulinā
tatkathaṃ ṣoḍaśavidhaṃ mahādānaṃ ca śobhanam
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ sūta buddhimatāṃvara
sūta uvāca
jīvacchrāddhaṃ purā kṛtvā manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prabhuḥ
tapasā ca vinītāya prahṛṣṭaḥ pradadau bhavaḥ
divyaṃ darśanamīśānas tenāpaśyat tam avyayam
natvā saṃpūjya vidhinā kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ sthitaḥ
pūjitaśca tato devo dṛṣṭaścaiva mayādhunā
śakraāya kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam
pūjitaś ca tato devo dṛṣṭaś caiva mayādhunā
śakraāya kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam
sūta uvāca
śrībhagavānuvāca
jayābhaṣekaṃ vakṣyāmi nṛpāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā
vidhinā maṇḍapaṃ kṛtvā prapāṃvā kūṭameva vā
navadhā stāpayedvahniṃ brāhmaṇo vedapāragaḥ
tataḥ sarvābhiṣekārthaṃ sūtrapātaṃ ca kārayet
prāgādyaṃ varṇasūtrañca dakṣiṇādyaṃ tathā punaḥ
sahasrāṇāṃ dvayaṃ tatra śatānāṃ ca catuṣṭayam
śeṣameva subhaṃ koṣṭhaṃ teṣu koṣṭhaṃ tu saṃharet
bāhye vīthyāṃ padañcaikaṃ samantādupasaṃharet
aṅgasūtrāṇi saṃgṛhya vidhinā pṛthageva tu
prāgādyaṃ varṇasūtraṃ ca dakṣiṇādyaṃ tathā punaḥ
prāgādyandakṣiṇādyaṃ ca ṣaṭtriśatsaṃharetkramāt
prāgādyāḥ paṅktayaḥ sapta dakṣiṇādyāstathā punaḥ
tasmādekonapañcāśatpaṅktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
kamalaṃ cālikhettatra hastāmātreṇa śobhanam
aṣṭapatraṃ sitaṃ vṛttaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam
aṣṭāṅgulapramāṇena karṇikā hemasannibhā
dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ ca yathākramam
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu sthāpayetpraṇavena tu
avyaktādīni vai dikṣu gātrākāreṇa vai nyaset
avyaktaṃ niyataḥ kālaḥ kālī ceti catuṣṭayam
sitaraktahiraṇyābhakṛṣṇā dharmādayaḥ kramāt
haṃsākāreṇa vai gātraṃ hemābhāsena suvratāḥ
ādhāraśaktimadhye tu kamalaṃ sṛṣṭikāraṇam
bindumātraṃ kalāmadhye nādākāramataḥ param
nādopari śivaṃ dhyāyedāeṅkārakhyaṃ jagadgurum
manonmanīṃ ca padmābhaṃmahādevaṃ ca bhāvayet
vāmādayaḥ krameṇaiva prāgādyāḥ kesareṣu vai
vāmā jyeṣṭhā tathā raudrī kālī vikaraṇī tathā
balā pramathinī devī damanī ca yathāṅkramam
namo 'stu vāmadevāya namo jyeṣṭhāya śūline
rudrāya kālarūpāya kalāvikaraṇāya ca
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śruṇu
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu
tṛtīyāvaraṇe caiva caturviśadanukramāt
piśāca vīrthirvai madhye nābhivīthiḥ samantataḥ
mantrairetairyathānyāyaṃ piśācānāṃ prakīrtitā
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ tu padamaṣṭārasaṃyutam
teṣuteṣu pṛthaktvena padeṣu kamalaṃ kramāt
kalpayecchālinīvāragodhūmaiśca yavādibhiḥ
taṇḍulaiśca tilairvātha gaurasarṣapasaṃyutaiḥ
athavā kalpayedetairyathākālaṃ vidhānataḥ
aṣṭapatraṃ likhetteṣu karṇikākesarānvitam
śālīnāmāḍhakaṃ proktaṃ kamalānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak
taṇḍulānāṃ tadardhaṃ syāttadardhaṃ ca yavādayaḥ
droṇaṃ pradhānakuṃbhasya tadardhaṃ taṇḍulāḥ smṛtāḥ
tilānāmāḍhakaṃ madhye yavānāṃ ca tadardhakam
athāṃbhasā samabhyukṣya kamalaṃ praṇavena tu
teṣu sarveṣu vidhinā praṇavaṃ vinyasetkramāt
kalaśānāṃ sahasrāṇi haimāni ca śubhāni ca
uktalakṣaṇayuktānu kārayedrājatāni vā
tāmrajāni yatānyāyaṃ praṇavenārghyavāriṇā
dvādaśāṅgulavistāramudare samudāhṛtam
kaṇṭhaṃ tu dvyaṅgulotsedhaṃ vistaraṃ caturaṅgulam
oṣṭhaṃ ca dvyaṅgulotsedhaṃ nirgamaṃ dvyagulaṃsmṛtam
yavāmātrāntaraṃ samyaktantunā veṣṭayeddhi vai
avaguṇṭhya tathābhyukṣya kuśopariyatāvidhi
pūrvavatpraṇavenaiva pūrayedgandhavāriṇā
sthāpayecchivakuṃbhāḍhyaṃ vardhanīṃ ca vidānataḥ
madhyapadmāsya madhye tu sakūrcaṃ sākṣataṃ kramāt
śivakuṃbhe śivaṃ sthāpya gāyatryā praṇaveja ca
vidmahaṃ puruṣāyaiva mahādevāya dhīmahi
vardhanyāṃ devigāyatryā devīṃ saṃsthāpya pūjayet
gaṇāṃbikāyai vidmahe mahātapāyai dhīmahi
prathamāvaraṇe caiva vāmādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śruṇu
śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaivātra pūrvādyānteṣu suvrata
bhadrāmāgneyacakre tu yāmye tu kanakāṇḍajām
aṃbikāṃ nairṛte vyūhe madhyakuṃbhe tu pūjayet
śrīdevīṃ vāruṇe bhāge vāgīśāṃ vāyugocare
eendrāgnividisormadhye pūjayedaṇimāṃ śubhām
vitteśānilayormadhye īśitvaṃ sthāpya pūjayet
vitteśeśānayormadhye vaśitvaṃ sthāpya pūjayet
eendreśeśānayormadhye yajetkāmāvasāyakam
dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ tṛtīyāvaraṇaṃ śuṇu
dīkṣāṃ dīkṣāyikāṃ caiva caṇḍāṃ caṇḍāṃśunāyikām
sumatiṃ sumatyāyīṃ ca gopāṃ gopāyikāṃ tathā
atha nandaṃ ca nandāyīṃ pitāmahamataḥ param
pitāmahāyīṃ pūrvādyaṃ vidhinā sthāpya pūjayet
erva saṃpūjya vidhinātṛtīyāvaraṇaṃ śubham
saubhadraṃ vyūhamāsādya prathamāvaraṇe kramāt
prāgādyaṃ vidhinā sthāpya śaktyaṣṭakamanukramāt
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva prāgādyaṃ śṛṇu śaktayaḥ
bindukā bindugarbhā ca nādinī nādagarbhajā
śaktikā śaktigarbhā ca parā caiva parāparā
pratamāvaraṇe 'ṣṭau ca śaktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
caṇḍā caṇḍamukhī caiva caṇḍavegā manojavā
caṇḍākṣīcaṇḍanirghoṣā bhṛkuṭī caṇḍanāyikā
manotsedhā manodhyakṣā mānasī mānanāyikā
manoharī manohlādī manaḥprītirmaheśvarī
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
saubhadraḥ kathito vyūho bhadraṃ vyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
eendrī hautāśanī yāmyā nairṛtī vāruṇī tathā
vāyavyā caiva kauberī aiśānī cāṣṭaśaktayaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
hariṇā ca suvarṇā ca kāñcanī hāṭakī tathā
rukmiṇī satyabhāmā ca subhagā jaṃbunāyikā
vāgbhavā vākpathā vāṇī bhīmā citrarathā sudhīḥ
vedamātā hiraṇyākṣī dvitīyāvaraṇe smṛtā
bhadrākhyaḥ kathito vyūhaḥ kanakākhyaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
vajraṃ śaktiṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ pāśaṃ dhvajaṃ tathā
gadāṃ triśulaṃ kramaśaḥ prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
yuddhā prabuddhā caṇḍā ca muṇḍā caiva kapālinī
mṛtyuhantrī virūpākṣī kapardā kamalāsanā
daṃṣṭriṇī raṅgiṇī caiva laṃbākṣī kaṅkabhūṣaṇī
saṃbhāvā bhāvinī caiva ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
kathitaḥ prathakavyūho hyambikākhyaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
khecarī cātmanā sā ca bhavānī vahnirūpiṇī
vahninī vahninābhā ca mahimāmṛtalālasā
prathamāvaraṇe cāṣṭau śaktayaḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
kṣamā ca śikharā devī ṛturatnā silā tathā
chāyā bhūtapanī dhanyā indramātā ca vaiṣṇavī
tṛṣṇā rāgavatī mohā kāmakopā mahotkaṭā
indrā ca badhirā devī ṣoḍaśaitāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
kathitaścāṃbikāvyūhaḥ śrīvyūhaṃ śṛṇu suvrata
svarśā svarśavatī gandhā prāṇāpānā samānikā
udānā vyānanāmā ca prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
tamohatā prabhāmoghā tejinī dahinī tathā
bhīmāsyā jālinī coṣā śoṣiṇī rudranāyikā
varibhadrā gaṇādhyakṣā candrahāsā ca gahvarā
gaṇamātāṃbikā caiva śaktayaḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
dvitīyāvaraṇe proktāḥ ṣoḍaśaiva yathākramāt
śrīvyūhaḥ kathito bhadraṃvāgīśaṃ śṛṇu suvrata
dhārā vāridharā caiva vahnikī nāśakī tathā
martyātītā mahāmāyā vajriṇī kāmadenukā
prathamāvaraṇe 'pyevaṃ śaktayo 'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ
payoṣṇī vāruṇī śāntā jayantī ca varapradā
plāvinī jalamātā ca payomātā mahāṃbikā
raktā karālī caṇḍākṣī mahocchuṣmā payasvinī
māyā vidyeśvarī kālī kālikā ca yathākramam
ṣoḍaśaiva samākhyātāḥ śaktayaḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
vyūho vāgīśvaraḥ prokto gomukho vyūha ucyate
śaṅkīnī hālinī caiva laṅkāvarṇā ca kalkinī
yakṣiṇī mālinī caiva vamanī ca rasātmanī
prathamāvaraṇe caiva śaktayo 'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ
caṇḍā ghaṇṭā mahānādā sumukhī durmukhī balā
revatī prathamā ghorā sainyā līnā mahābalā
jayā ca vijayā caiva aparā cāparājitā
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu
kathito gomukhīvyūho bhadrakarṇī śṛṇuṣva me
mahājayā virupākṣī śuklābhākāśamātṛkā
saṃhāri jātahārī ca daṃṣṭrālī suṣkarevatī
prathamāvaraṇe cāṣṭau śaktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
pipīlikā puṇyahārī aśanī sarvahāriṇī
bhadrahā viśvahārī ca himāyogeśvarī tathā
chidrā bhānumatī chidrā saiṃhikī surabhī samā
sarvabhavyā ca vegākhyā śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu
mahāvyūhāṣṭakaṃ proktamupavyuhāṣṭakaṃ śṛṇu
aṇimāvyūhamāveṣṭya prathamāvaraṇe kramāt
eendrā tu citrabhānuśca vāruṇī daṇḍireva ca
prāṇarūpī tathā haṃsaḥ svātmaśaktiḥ pitāmahaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
mahātmā ca tathā hyātmā hyantarātmā maheśvaraḥ
paramātmāṃ hyaṇurjīvaḥ piṅgalaḥ puruṣaḥ paśuḥ
bhoktā bhūtapatirbhīmo dvitīyāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
kathitaścāṇimāvyūho laghimākhyaṃ vadāmi te
śrīkaṇṭhāentaśca sūkṣmaśca trimūrtiḥ śaśakastathā
amareśaḥ sthitīśaśca dārataśca tathāṣṭamaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
sthāṇurharaśca daṇḍeśo bhauktīśaḥ surapuṅgavaḥ
sadyojāto 'nugraheśaḥ krūrasenaḥ sureśvaraḥ
krodhīśaśca tathā caṇḍaḥ pracaṇḍaḥ śiva eva ca
dvitīyāvaraṇe rudrāḥ ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
kathito laghimāvyūho mahimāṃ śṛṇusuvrata
ajeśaḥ kṣemarudraśca somoṃ'śau lāṅgalī tathā
daṇḍāruścārdhanārī ca ekāntaścānta eva ca
pālī bhujaṅganāmā ca pinākī khaḍkireva ca
kāma īśastathā śveto bhṛguḥ ṣoḍaśa vai smṛtāḥ
kathito mahimāvyūhaḥ prāptivyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣva mai
saṃvarto lakulīśaśca vāḍavo hastireva ca
caṇḍayakṣo gaṇapatirmahātmā bhṛgujo 'ṣṭamaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
trivikramo mahājihvo ṛkṣaḥ śrībhadra eva ca
mahādevo dadhīcaśca kumāraśca parāvaraḥ
mahādaṃṣṭraḥ karālaśca sūcakaśca suvardhanaḥ
mahādhvāṅkṣo mahānando daṇḍī gopālakastathā
prāptivyūhaḥ samākhyātaḥ prākāmyaṃ śṛṇu suvrata
puṣpadanto mahānāgo vipulānandakārakaḥ
śuklo viśālaḥ kamalo bilvaścāruma eva ca
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śruṇu
ratipriyaḥ sureśānaścitrāṅgaśca sudurjayaḥ
vināyakaḥ kṣetrapālo mahāmohaśca jaṅgalaḥ
sarvāvasthādhipo devo meghanādaḥ pracaṇḍakaḥ
kāladūtaśca kathito dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ smṛtam
prākāmyaḥ kathito vyūha aiśvaryaṃ kathayāmi te
maṅgalā carcikā caiva yogeśā haradāyikā
bhāsurā suramātā ca suṃdarī mātṛkāṣṭamī
prathamāvaraṇe proktā dvitīyāvaraṇe śṛṇu
gaṇādhipaśca mantrajño varadevaḥ ṣaḍānanaḥ
aśvīrudraśca someśaścottamoduṃbarastathā
apāṃpatiśca vidhinā dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ smṛtam
mahājayastathāṃ gāro vyaṅgāraśca mahāyaśāḥ
prathamāvaraṇe proktā dvitīyāvaraṇe śṛṇu
suṃdaraśca pracaṇḍeśo mahāvarṇo mahāsuraḥ
mahāromā mahāgarbhaḥ prathamaḥ kanakastathā
vaśitvaṃ kathito vyūhaḥ śṛṇu kāmāvasāyikam
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
dharmaścātibalaḥ sarpo mahākāyo mahāhanuḥ
vajraḥ kālāgnirudraśca sadyonādo mahāguhaḥ
dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ vyūhaścaivāvasāyikaḥ
kathitaḥ ṣoḍaśo vyūho dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva dakṣavyūhe ca śaktayaḥ
prathamāvaraṇe cāṣṭau bāhye ṣoḍaśa eva ca
manoharā mahānādā citrā citrarathā tathā
rohiṇī caiva citrāṅgī citrarekhā vicitrikā
prathamāvaraṇe proktā dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
citrā vicitrarūpā ca śubhadā kāmadā subhā
krūrā ca piṅgalā devī khaḍgikā laṃbikāsatī
daṃṣṭrālī rākṣasīdhvaṃsī lolupā lohitāmukhī
dvitīyāvaraṇe proktoḥ ṣoḍaśaiva samāsataḥ
dakṣavyūhaḥ samākhyāto dākṣavyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
sarvāsatī viśvarūpā laṃpaṭā cāmiṣapriyā
dīrghadaṃṣṭrā ca vajrā ca laṃboṣṭhī prāṇahāriṇī
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
gajakarṇāśvakarṇā ca mahākālī subhīṣaṇa
vātavegaravā ghorā ghānāghanaravā tathā
varaghoṣā mahāvarṇā sughaṇṭā ghaṇṭikā tathā
ghaṇṭaśvarī mahāghorā ghorā caivātighorikā
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
dākṣavyūhaḥ samākhyātaścāṇḍavyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣvame
atighaṇṭā cātighorā karālā karabhā tathā
vibhūtirbhogadā kāntiḥ śaṅkhinī cāṣṭamī smṛtā
prathamāvaraṇe proktā dvitīyāvaraṇe śṛṇu
patriṇī caiva gāndhārī yogamātā supīvarā
raktā mālāṃśukā vīrā saṃhārī māṃsahāriṇī
phalahārī jīvahārī svecchāhārī ca tuṇḍikā
revatī raṅgiṇī saṃgā dvitīye ṣoḍaśaiva tu
caṇḍavyūhaḥ samākhyātaścaṇḍāvyūhastathocyate
caṇḍī caṇḍamukhī caṇḍā caṇḍavegā mahāravā
bhrukuṭī caṇḍabhūścaiva caṇḍarūpāṣṭamī smṛtā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
candraghrāṇā balā caiva balajihvā baleśvarī
balavegā mahākāyā mahākopā ca vidyutā
kaṅkālī kalaśī caiva vidyutā caṇḍaghoṣikā
mahāghoṣā mahārāvā caṇḍabhānaṅgacaṇḍikā
caṇḍāyāḥ kathito vyūho haravyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
caṇḍākṣī kāmadā devī sūkarī kukkuṭānanā
gāndhārī dandubhī durgā saumitrā cāṣṭamī smṛtā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
mṛtodbhavā mahālakṣmīrvarṇadā jīvarakṣiṇī
hariṇī kṣīṇajīvā ca daṇḍavaktrā caturbhujā
vyomacārī vyomarūpā vyomavyāpī śubhodayā
gṛhacārī sucārī ca viṣāhārī viṣartihā
haravyūhaḥ samākhyāto harāyā vyūha ucyate
jaṃbhācyutā ca kaṅkārī devikā durdharāvahā
caṇḍikā capalā ceti prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
cañjikā cāmarī caiva bhaṇḍikā ca śubhānanā
piṇḍikā muṇḍikā muṇḍā śākinī śāṅkarī tathā
kartarī bhartarī caiva bhāginī yajñadāyinī
yamadaṃṣṭrā mahādaṃṣṭrā karālā ceti śaktayaḥ
harāyāḥ kathito vyūhaḥ śaiṇḍavyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
vikarālī karālī ca kālajaṅghā yaśasvinī
vegā vegavatī yajñā vedāṅgā cāṣṭamī smṛtā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
vajrā śaṅkhātiśaṅkhā vā balā caivābalā tathā
añjanī mohinī māyā vikaṭāṅgī nalī tathā
gaṇḍakī daḍakī ghoṇā śoṇā satyavatī tathā
kallolā ceti ṛmaśaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva yathāvidhi
śaiṇḍavyūhaḥ samākhyātaḥ śaiṇḍāyā vyūha ucyate
danturā raudrabhāgā ca amṛtā sakulā śubhā
calajihvāryanetrā ca rūpiṇī dārikā tathā
prathamā varaṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
khādikā rūpanāmā ca saṃhārī ca kṣamāntakā
kaṇḍinī peṣiṇī caiva mahātrāsā kṛtāntikā
daṇḍinī kiṅkarī biṃbā varṇinī cāmalāṅginī
draviṇī drāviṇī caiva śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu
kathito hi manoramyaḥ śauṇḍāyā vyūha uttamaḥ
prathamākhyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vyūhaṃ paramaśobhanam
plavinī plāvanī śobhā mandā caiva madotkaṭā
mandākṣepā mahādevī prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
kāmasaṃdīpinī devī atirūpā manoharā
mahāvaśā mahāgrāhā vihvalā madavihvalā
aruṇā śoṣaṇā divyā revatī bhāṇḍanāyikā
staṃbhinī ghoraraktākṣī smararūpā sughoṣaṇā
vyūhaḥ prathama ākhyātaḥ svāyaṃbhuva yathā tathā
kathitaṃ prathamavyūhaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva me
ghorā ghoratarāghorā atighorāghanāyikā
dhāvanī kroṣṭukā muṇḍā cāṣṭamī parikīrtitā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
bhīmā bhīmatarā bhīmā śastā caiva suvartulā
staṃbhinī rodanī raudrā rudravatyacalā calā
mahābalā mahāśāntiḥ śālā śāntā śivāśivā
bṛhatkakṣā mahānāsā ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
prathamāyāḥ samākhyāto manmathavyūha ucyate
tālakarṇī ca bālā ca kalyāṇī kapilā śivā
iṣṭistuṣṭiḥ pratijñā ca prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
khyātiḥ puṣṭikarī tuṣṭirjalā caiva śrutirdhṛtiḥ
kāmadā śubhadā saumyā tejinī kāmatantrikā
dharmā dharmavaśā śīlā pāpahā dharmavardhinī
manmathaḥ kathito vyūho manmathāyāḥ śṛṇuṣva me
dharmarakṣā vidhānā ca dharmā dharmavatī tathā
sumatirdurmatirmedhā vimalā cāṣṭamī smṛtā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
balā cātibalā bhīmā prāṇavṛddhikarī tathā
nirlajjā nirghṛṇā mandā sarvapāpakṣayaṅkarī
kapilā cātividhurā ṣoḍaśaitāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
kāmā tṛṣṇā kṣudhā mohā cāṣṭamī parikīrtitā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śruṇu
jayā nidrā bhayālasyā jalatṛṣṇodarī darā
kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇāṅginī vṛddhā śuddhocchiṣṭāśanī vṛṣā
kāmanā śobhinī dagdhā duḥkhadā sukhadāvalī
bhīmavyūhaḥ samākhyāto bhīmāyīvyūha ucyate
ānandā ca sunandā ca mahānandā subhaṅkarī
vatirāgā mahotsāhā jitarāgā manoratā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śuṇu
manonmanī manaḥkṣobhā madonmattā gadākulā
mandagārbhā mahābhāsā kāmānandā suvuhvalā
mahāvegā suvegā ca mahābhogā kṣayāvahā
kramiṇī kramiṇī vakraā dvitīyāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
kathitaṃ tava bhīmāyīvyūhaṃ paramaśobhanam
śākunaṃ kathayāmyādya svāyaṃbhuva manotsukam
yogā vegā suvegā ca ativegā suvāsinī
devī manorayā vegā jalāvartā ca dhīmatī
prathamāvaraṃṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
rodhinī kṣobhiṇī bālā viprāśeṣāsuśoṣiṇī
vidyutā bhāsinī devī manovegā ca cāpalā
vidyujjihvā mahājihvā bhṛkuṭīkuṭilānanā
phullajvālā mahājvālā sujvālā ca kṣayāntikā
śākunaḥ kathito vyūhaḥ śākunāyāḥ śṛṇuṣvame
jvālinī caiva bhasmāṅgī tathā bhasmāntagā tatā
bhāvinī ca prajā vidyā khyātiścaivāṣṭamī smṛtā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
ullekhā ca patākā ca bhogābhogavatī khagā
bhogabhogavratā yogā bhogākhyā yogapāragā
ṛddhirbuddhirdhṛtiḥ kāntiḥ smṛtiḥ sākṣācchrutirdharā
śākunāyā mahāvyūhaḥ kathitaḥ kāmadāyakaḥ
svāyaṃbhuva śṛṇu vyūhaṃ sumatyākhyaṃ suśobhanam
pareṣṭā ca parā dṛṣṭā hyamṛtā phalanāśinī
hiraṇyākṣī suvarṇākṣī devī sākṣātkapiñjalā
kāmarekhā ca kathitaṃ prathamāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
ratnadvīpā ca sudvīpā ratnadā ratnamālinī
ratnaśobhā suśobhā ca mahāśobhā mahādyutiḥ
śāṃbarī bandhurā granthiḥ pādakarṇā karānanā
hayagrīvā ca jihvā ca sarvabhāsoti śaktayaḥ
sarvāśī ca mahābhakṣā mahādaṃṣṭrātirauravā
visphuliṅgā viliṅgāca kṛtāntā bhāskarānanā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
rāgā raṅgāvatī śreṣṭhā mahākrodhā ca rauravā
nālī sunālī saumyā ca ityevaṃ kathitaṃ mayā
gopavyūhaṃ vadāmyatra śṛṇu svāyaṃbhuvākhilam
pāṭalī pāṭavī caiva pāṭī vidipiṭā tathā
kaṅkaṭā supaṭā caiva praghaṭā ca ghaṭodbhavā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ cātra bhāṣayā kathitaṃ mayā
nādākṣī nādarūpā ca sarvakārī gamāgamā
anucārī sucārī ca caṇḍanāḍī suvāhinī
suyogā ca viyogā ca haṃsākhyā ca vilāsinī
sarvagā suvicārā ca vañcanī ceti śaktayaḥ
gopavyūhaḥ samākhyāto gopāyīvyūha ucyate
bhedinī ccedinī caiva sarvakārī kṣudhāśanī
ucchuṣmā caiva gāndhārī bhasmāśī vaḍavānalā
prathamāvaraṇaṃ caiva dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
andhā bāhvāsinī bālā dīkṣapāmā tathaiva ca
akṣātryakṣā ca hṛllekhā hṛdgatā māyikāparā
āmayāsādinībhillī sahyāsahyā sarasvatī
gopāyī kathito vyūho nandavyūhaṃ vadāmi te
nandinī ca nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca yathākramam
vidyānāsā khagrasinī cāmuṇḍā priyadarśinī
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
gṛhyā nārāyaṇī mohā prajā devī ca cakriṇī
kaṅkaṭā ca tathā kālī śivādyoṣā tataḥ param
virāmā yā ca vāgīśī vāhinībhīṣaṇī tathā
sugamā caiva nirdiṣṭā dvitayivaraṇe smṛtā
nandavyūho mayā khyāto nandāyā vyūha ucyate
vināyakī pūrṇimā ca raṅkārī kuṇḍalī tathā
icchā kapālinī caiva dvīpinī ca jayantikā
prathamāvaraṇe cāṣṭau śaktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
pāvanī cāṃbikā caiva sarvātmā pūtanā tathā
chagalī modinī sākṣāddevī laṃbodarī tathā
saṃhāri kālinī caiva kusumā ca yatākramam
śukraā tārā tathā jñānā kriyā gāyatrikā tathā
sāvitrī ceti vidhinā dvitīyā varaṇaṃ smṛtam
nandāyāḥ kathito vyūhaḥ paitāmahamataḥ param
nandinī caiva phetkārī krodhā haṃsā ṣaḍaṅgulā
ānandā vasudurgā ca saṃhārā hyamṛtāṣṭamī
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
kulāntikānalā caiva pracaṇḍā mardinī tathā
sarvabhūtābhayā caiva dayā ca vaḍavāmukhī
laṃpaṭā pannagā devī kusumā vipulāntakā
kedārā ca tathā kūrmā duritā mandarodarī
khaḍgacakrotividhinā dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ smṛtam
vyūhaḥ paitāmahaḥ prokto dharmakāmārthamuktidaḥ
pitāmahāyā vyūhaṃ ca kathayāmi śṛṇuṣva me
vajrā ca nandanā śāvarāvikā ripubhedinī
rūpā caturthā yogā ca prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
bhūtā nādā mahābālā kharparā ca tathā parā
bhasmā kāntā tathā vṛṣṭirdvibhujā brahmarūpiṇī
saihyā vaikārikā jātā karmamoṭī tathāparā
mahāmohā mahāmāyā gāndhārī puṣpamālinī
śabdāpī ca mahāghoṣā ṣoḍaśaiva tathāntime
sarvāśca dvibhujā devyo bālabhāskarasannibhāḥ
padmaśaṅkhadharāḥ śāntā raktasragvastrabhūṣaṇāḥ
sarvābharaṇasaṃpūrṇā mukuṭādyairalaṅkṛtāḥ
vibhūṣitā gauravarṇādhyeyā devyaḥ pṛthakpṛthak
evaṃ sahasrakalaśaṃ tāmrajaṃ mṛnmayaṃ tu vā
pūrvoktalakṣaṇairyuktaṃ rudrakṣetre pratiṣṭhitam
bhavādyairviṣṇunā proktairnāmnāṃ caiva sahasrakaiḥ
catvāriṃśanmahāvyūhaṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam
sarveṣāṃ kalaśaṃ proktaṃ pūrvavaddhemanirmitam
sarve gandhāṃbusaṃpūrṇapañcaratnasamanvitāḥ
tathā kanakasaṃyuktā devasya ghṛtapūritāḥ
kṣīreṇa vātha dadhnā vā pañcagavyena vā punaḥ
rudrādhyāyena rudrasya nṛpateḥśṛṇu sattama
mantreṇānena rājānaṃ secayedabhiṣecitam
homaṃ ca mantraṇānena aghoreṇāghahāriṇā
prāgādyaṃ devakuṇḍe vā sthāṇḍile vā ghṛtādibhiḥ
samidājyacaruṃ lājaśālinīvārataṇḍulaiḥ
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā rājānamadhivāsayet
bhasitaṃ ca mṛṇālena bandhayeddakṣiṇe kare
urvārukamiva bandhanān mṛtyor mukṣīya māmṛtāt
mantreṇānena rājānaṃ secayedvātha homayet
svāhāntaṃ puruṣeṇaivaṃ prākkuṇḍaṃ homayoddvijaḥ
aghoreṇa ca yāmye ca homayetkṛṣṇavāsasā
vāmadevāya namo jyeṣṭhāya namaḥ śreṣṭhāya namo rudrāya namaḥ
sadyojātaṃ prapadyāmi sadyojātāya vai namaḥ
svāhādaṃ juhuyādagnau mantreṇānena buddhimān
āgneyyāṃ ca vidhānena ṛcā raudreṇa homayet
nimi niśi diśa svāhā khaḍga rākṣasa bhedana
rudhirājyārdra nairṛtyai svāhā namaḥ svadhānamaḥ
yamyāṃ hi vividhairdravyairīśānena dvijottamāḥ
iśānāya kadrudrāya pracetase tryaṃbakāya śarvāya tanno rudraḥ pracodayāt
pradhānaṃ pūrvavaddravyairīśānena dvijottamāḥ
svayaṃ vā juhuyādagnau bhūpatiḥ śivātsalaḥ
īśānaḥ sarvavidyānāmīśvīraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmādhipatirbrahmaṇo 'dhipatirbrahmā śivo me astu sadā śivom
prāyāścittamaghoreṇa śeṣaṃ sāmānyamācaret
kṛtādhivāsaṃ rājānaṃ śaṅkhabheryādinisvanaiḥ
rudrādhyāyena vidhinā rudrabhasmāṅgadhāriṇam
śibikāṃ vaijayantīṃ ca sādhayennṛpateḥ śubhām
rājyābhiṣekayuktāya kṣatriyāyeśvarāya vā
nṛpacihnāni nānyeṣāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ vidhīyate
pramāṇaṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ dvādaśāṅgulamucyate
palāśoduṃbarāśvatthavaṭāḥ pūrvāditaḥ kramāt
toraṇādyāni vai tatra paṭṭamātreṇa paṭṭikāḥ
aṣṭamāṅgulasaṃyuktadarbhamālāsamāvṛtam
digdhvajāṣṭakasaṃyuktaṃ dvārakuṃbhaiḥ suśobhanam
hematoraṇakuṃbhaiśca bhūṣitaṃ snāpayennṛpam
tanmaheśāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi
tannaḥ śivaḥ pracodayāt
mantreṇānena vidhinā vardhanyā gaurigītayā
rudrādhyāyena vā sarvamaghorāyātha vā punaḥ
divyairābharaṇaiḥ śuklairmukuṭādyaiḥ sukalpitaiḥ
kṣaumavastraiśca rājānaṃ toṣayenniyataṃ śanaiḥ
aṣṭaṣaṣṭipalenaiva hemnā kṛtvā sudarśanam
navaratnairalaṅkṛtya dadyādvai dakṣiṇāḥ guroḥ
śatadroṇatilaṃ caiva śatadroṇāṃśca taṇḍulān
śayanaṃ vāhanaṃ śayyāṃ sopadhānāṃ pradāpayet
yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ triṃśatpalamudāhṛtam
aśeṣāṃśca tadardhena śivabhaktāṃstadardhataḥ
mahāpūjāṃ tataḥ kuryānmahādevasya vai nṛpaḥ
evaṃ purābhiṣiktastu śakraḥ śakratvamāgataḥ
brahmā brahmatvamāpanno viṣṇurviṣṇutvamāgataḥ
aṃbikā cāṃbikātvaṃ ca saubhāgyamatulaṃ tathā
sāvitrī ca tathā lakṣmīrdevī kātyāyanī tathā
nandinātha purā mṛtyū rudrādhyāyena vai jitaḥ
abhiṣikto 'suraḥ pūrvaṃ tārakākhyo mahābalaḥ
vidyunmālī hiraṇyākṣo viṣṇunā vai vinirjitaḥ
nṛsiṃhena purā daityo hiraṇyakaśipurhataḥ
skandena tārakādyāśca kauśikyā ca purāṃbayā
prāptāśca siddhayo divyānātra kāryā vicāraṇā
aho 'bhiṣekamāhātmyamaho śuddhasubhāṣitam
kalpakoṭiśatenāpi yatpāpaṃ samupārjitam
snātvaivaṃ mucyate rājā sarvapāpairna saṃśayaḥ
vyādhito mucyate rājā kṣayakuṣṭhādibhiḥ punaḥ
janānurāgasaṃpanno devarāja ivāparaḥ
modate pāpahīnaśca priyayā dharmaniṣṭhayā
nṛpāṇāmupakārāya svāyaṃbhuva mano mayā
iti śrīliṃṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge abhiṣekavidhirnāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
divyena cakṣuṣārudrāṃ nīlalohitamīśvaram
dṛṣṭvā tuṣṭāva varadaṃ rudrādhyāyena śaṅkaram
devo 'pi tuṣṭyā nirvāṇaṃ rājyānte karmaṇaiva tu
tavā stīti sakṛccoktvā tatraivāntaradhīyata
āruroha mahāmeruṃ mahāvṛṣamiveśvaraḥ
namaścakāra varadaṃ brahmaṇyaṃ brahmarūpiṇam
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā tuṣṭāva ca mahādyutiḥ
so 'pi dṛṣṭvā manuṃ devo hṛṣṭaromābhavanmuniḥ
sanatkumāraḥ prāhedaṃ ghṛṇayā ca ghṛṇānidhe
dṛṣṭvā sarveśvarācchāntācchaṅkarānnīlalohitāt
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
vijñāpayāmāsa kathaṃ karmaṇā nirvṛtirvibho
jñānena nirvṛtiḥ siddhā vibho miśreṇa vā kkacit
atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā śrutisāravidāṃ nidhiḥ
sanatkumāro bhagavānkarmaṇā nirvṛtiṅkramāt
miśreṇa ca kramādeva kṣaṇājjñānena vai mune

sviṣṭāntaṃ sarvakāryāṇi kārayedvidhivattadā

sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
agna āyūṃṣi pavasa āsuvorjamiṣaṃ ca naḥ
agnirṛṣiḥ pavamānaḥ pāñcajanyaḥ purohitaḥ
prajāpate na tvadetānyanyo viśvājātāni paritā babhūva
caruṇā ca tathājyasya śakradīnāṃ ca homayet
vajrādīnāṃ ca hotavyaṃ sahasrārdhaṃ tataḥ kramāt
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsu devāya dhīmahi
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt

dūrvayā kṣīrayuktena pañcaviṃśatpṛthakpṛthak
urvārukam iva bandhanān mṛtyormukṣayi māmṛtāt
dūrvāhomaḥ praśasto 'yaṃ vāsuhomaśca sarvathā
prāyaścittamaghoreṇa sarpiṣā ca śataṃśatam
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe vāme viṣṇuṃ viśvaguruṃ śivam
madhye devyā samaṃ jñeyamindrādigaṇasaṃvṛtam
ādityaṃ bhāskaraṃ bhānuṃ raviṃ devaṃ divākaram
uṣāṃ prabhāṃ tathā prajñāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sāvitrimeva ca
viṣṭarāṃ subhagāṃ caiva vardhanīṃ ca pradakṣiṇām
āpyāyanīṃ ca saṃpūjya devī padmāsane ravim
prabhūtaṃ vātha kartavyaṃ vimalaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā
sāraṃ paścimabhāge ca ārādhyaṃ cottare yajet
madhye sukhaṃ vijānīyātkesareṣu yathākramam
dīptāṃ sūkṣmāṃ jayāṃ bhadrāṃ vibhūtiṃ vimalāṃ kramāt
bhārgavaṃ ca tathā mandaṃ rāhuṃ ketuṃ tathaiva ca
pūjayeddhomayedevaṃ dāpayecca viśeṣataḥ
dārayettatra bhūpālaṃ ghaṭikaikāṃ vidānataḥ
ghaṭikārdhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā tatraivāsanāmārabhet
ālokya vāruṇaṃ dhīmānkūrcahastaḥ samāhitaḥ
nṛpaśca bhūṣaṇairyuktaḥ khaḍgakheṭakadhārakaḥ
svastirityādibhiścādāvante caiva viśeṣataḥ
puṇyāhaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ kāryaṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ
jayamaṅgalaśabdādibrahmaghoṣaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ
nṛtyavādyādibhirgītaiḥ sarvaśobhāsamanvitaiḥ
tulādhārau samau vṛttau tulābhāraḥ sadā bhavet
śataniṣkādhikaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tadardhaṃ madhyamaṃ smṛtam
vastrayugmamathoṣṇīṣaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ kaṇṭhaśobhanam
aṅgulībhīṣaṇaṃ caiva maṇibandhasya bhūṣaṇam
etāni caiva sarvāṇi prāraṃbhe dharmakarmaṇi
pāśupatavratāyātha bhasmāṅgāya pradāpayet
pūrvoktabhūṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ soṣṇīṣaṃ vastrasaṃyutam
dakṣiṇāṃ ca śataṃ sārdhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā pradāpayet
yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ pṛthaṅniṣkaṃ pradāpayet
yāgopakaraṇaṃ divyamācāryāya pradāpayet
itareṣāṃ yatīnāṃ tu pṛthaṅniṣkaṃ pradāpayet
prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ caiva prākāraṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ tathā
suvarṇapuṣpaṃ paṭahaṃ khaḍgaṃ vai kośameva ca
kṛtvā dattvā śivāyātha kiñciccheṣaṃ ca buddhimān
ācāryebhyaḥ pradātavyaṃ bhasmāṅgebhyo viśeṣataḥ
payasā vātha dadhnā vā sarvadravyairathāpi vā
payasā vātha dadhnā vā sarvadravyairathāpi vā
brahmakūrcena vā devaṃ pañcagavyena vā punaḥ
gāyatryā caiva gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ praṇavena vā
āpyāyasveti vai kṣīraṃ dadhikraāvṇoti vai dadhi
tejosītyājyamīśānamantreṇaivābhiṣecayet
devasyatvoti deveśaṃ kuśāṃbukalaśena vai
sahasrakalaśaṃ śaṃbhornāmnāṃ caiva sahasrakaiḥ
viṣṇunā kathitairvāpi taṇḍinā kathitaistu vā
mahāpūjā prakartavyā mahādevasya bhaktitaḥ
śivārcakāya dātavyā dakṣiṇā svaguroḥ sadā
dehārṇavaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ dakṣiṇā ca yatākramam
dīnāndhakṛpaṇānāṃ ca bālavṛddhakṛsāturān
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tulāpuruṣadānavidhāvaṣṭāviṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
tulā te kathitā hyeṣā ādyā sāmānyarūpiṇī
adhaḥ pātraṃ sahasreṇa hiraṇyena vidhīyate
ūrdhvapātraṃ tadardhena mukhaṃ saṃveśamātrakam
haimamevaṃ śubhaṃ kuryāt sarvālaṃkārasaṃyutam
adhaḥ pātre smareddevīṃ guṇatrayasamanvitām
caturviśatikāṃ devīṃ brahmaviṣṇvagnirūpiṇīm
ūrdhvapātre guṇātītaṃ ṣaḍviśakamumāpatim
ātmānaṃ puruṣaṃ dhyāyetpañcaviśakamagrajam
śālīmadhye kṣipennītvā navavastraiśca veṣṭayet
māṣakalkena cāliṣya pañcadravyeṇa pūjayet
īśānādyairyathānyāyaṃ pañcabhiḥ paripūjayet
devīṃ gāyatrikāṃ japtvā praviśetprāṅmukhaḥ svayam
vidhinaiva tu saṃpādya garbhādhānādikāṃ kriyām
kṛtvā ṣoḍaśamārgeṇa vidhinā brāhmaṇottamaḥ
dūrvākuraistu kartavyā secanā dakṣiṇe puṭe
īśānyāṃ tāvadevātra kuryātsīmantakarmaṇi
udvahetkanyakāṃ kṛtvā triṃśanniṣkeṇa śobhanām
alaṅkṛtya tathā hutvā śivāya vinivedayet
annaprāśanake vidvān bhojayetpāyasādibhiḥ
evaṃ viśvajitāntā vai garbhādhānādikāḥ kriyāḥ
śaktibījena kartavyā brāhmaṇairvedapāragaiḥ
śeṣaṃ sarvaṃ ca vidhivattulāhemavadācaret
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
pūrvoktasthānakāle tu kṛtvā saṃpūjya yatnataḥ
daśatālapramāṇaena daṇḍaṃ saṃsthāpya vai mune
adbhiḥ saṃprokṣya paścāddhi tilāṃstvasminvinikṣipet
pañcagavyena taṃ deśaṃ prokṣayedbrāhmaṇottamaḥ
tasminsaṃcayanaṃ kāryaṃ tilabhārairviśeṣataḥ
daṇḍaprādeśamutsedhamuttamaṃ parikīrtitam
caturaṅgulahīnaṃ tu madhyamaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
daṇḍatulyaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ syāddaṇḍahīnaṃ na kārayet
veṣṭayitvā navairvastraiḥ paritaḥ pūjayetkramāt
aṣṭadikṣu ca kartavyāḥ pūrvoktā mūrtayaḥ kramāt
dakṣiṇā vidhinā kāryā tulābhāravadeva tu
śivārcanā ca kartavyā sahasrakalaśādibhiḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tilaparvatadānaṃ nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
athānyaṃ parvataṃ sūkṣmamalpadravyaṃ mahāphalam
gomayāliptabhūmau tu hyaṃbarāṇi prakīrya ca
tanmadhye nikṣipeddhīmāṃstilabhāratrayaṃ śubham
padmamaṣṭadalaṃ kuryātkarṇikākesarānvitam
daśaniṣkeṇa tatkāryaṃ tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
ārādhya vidhivaddevaṃ vāmādīni prapūjayet
śaktirūpaṃ suvarṇena triniṣkeṇa tu kārayet
nyāsaṃ tu paritaḥ kuryādvighneśānparibhāgataḥ
tān abhyarcya vidhānena gandhapūṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
japahomārcanādānābhiṣekādyaṃ ca pūrvavat
muvarṇamedinīdānaṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ
lakṣaṇena yathāpūrvaṃ kuṇḍe vā maṇḍale 'tha vā
medinīṃ kārayeddivyāṃ sahasreṇāpi vā punaḥ
pūrvavannikilaṃ kṛtvā maṇḍale vedimadhyataḥ
śivabhakte pradātavyā dakṣiṇā pūrvacoditā
sahasrakalaśādyaiśca śaṅkaraṃ pūjayecchivam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge suvarṇamedinīnīdānaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śatāniṣkeṇa kṛtvaivaṃ sarvaśākhāsamanvitam
śākhānāṃ vividhaṃ kṛtvā muktā dāmādyalaṃbanam
vaiḍūryeṇa drumāgraṃ ca puṣparāgeṇa mastakam
candrakāntena vā vedīṃ drumasya sphaṭikena vā
vitastimātramāyāmaṃ vṛkṣasya parikīrtitam
śākhāṣṭakasya mānaṃ ca vistāraṃ cordhvatastathā
tanmūle stāpayelliṅgaṃ lokapālaiḥ samāvṛtam
pūjaye ddevamīśānaṃ lokapālāṃśca yatnataḥ
pūrvavajjapahomādyaṃ tulābhāravadācaret
nivedayeddrumaṃ śaṃbhoryogināṃ vātha vā nṛpa
bhasmāṅgibhyo 'thavā rājā sārvabhaumo bhaviṣyati
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kalpapādapadānavidirnāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
gaṇeśeśaṃ pravakṣyāmi dānaṃ pūrvoktamaṇḍape
saṃpūjya devadevesaṃ lokapālasamāvṛtam
viśveśvarānyathāśāstraṃ sarvābharaṇasaṃyutān
daśaniṣkeṇa vai kṛtvā saṃpūjya ca vidhānataḥ
aṣṭadakṣvaṣṭakuṇḍeṣu pūrvavaddhomamācaret
pañcāvaraṇamārgeṇa pāraṃparyakrameṇa ca
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge gaṇeśeśadānavidinirūpaṇaṃ nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ grahadurbhikṣanāśanam
niṣkāṇāṃ ca sahasreṇa suvarṇena tu kārayet
śatena vā prakartavyā sarvarūpaguṇānvitā
gorūpaṃ sukhuraṃ divyaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
vauḍūryeṇa stanāḥ kāryā lāṅgūlaṃ nīlataḥ subham
dantasthāne prakartavyaḥ puṣparāgaḥ suśobhanaḥ
paśuvatkārayitvā tu vatsaṃ kuryātsuśobhanam
saṃpūjayedgāṃ gāyatryā savatsāṃ surabhiṃ punaḥ
śivapūjā prakartavyā liṅgaṃ snāpya ghṛtādibhiḥ
gāmālabhya ca gāyatryā śivāyādāpayecchubhām
dakṣiṇā ca prakartavyā triṃśanniṣkā mahāmate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hemadhenudānavidhinīrūpaṇaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
lakṣmīdānaṃ pravakṣyāmi mahadaiśvaryavardhanam
pūrvoktamaṇḍapekāryaṃ vedikoparimaṇḍale
śrīdevīmatulāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi
aṣṭottaraśatenāpi sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām
maṇḍale vinyasellakṣmīṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutām
tasyāstu dakṣiṇe bhāge sthaṇḍile viṣṇumarcayet
arcayitvā vidhānena śrīsuktena sureśvarīm
arcayedviṣṇugāyatryā viṣṇuṃ viśvaguruṃ harim
ārādhya vidhinā devīṃ pūrvavaddhoma mācaret
pṛthagaṣṭotaraśataṃ homayed brāhmaṇottamaiḥ
āhūya yajamānaṃ tu tasyāḥ pūrvadiśi sthale
tasmai tāṃ darśayeddevīṃ daṇḍavatpraṇamotkṣitau
praṇamya viṣṇuṃ tatrasthaṃ śivaṃ pūrvavadarcayet
tasyā viṃśatibhāgaṃ tu dakṣiṇā parikīrtitā
tadardhāṃśaṃ tu dātavyamitareṣāṃ yathārhataḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge lakṣmīdānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumārā uvāca
pūrvoktamaṇḍape kuryācchivapūjāṃ tu paścime
tilapuṣpaṃ tu kṛtvātha hemapadmaṃ vinikṣipet
triṃśanniṣkema kartavyaṃ tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
pañcaniṣkeṇa kartavyaṃ tadardhārhdena vā punaḥ
tamārādhya vidhānena gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
ācchādanottarāsaṃgaṃ viprebhyo dāpayetkramāt
uṣṇīṣaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ kuṇḍaleca vibhūṣite
hemāṅgulīyakaṃ dattvā brāhmaṇebhyo vidhānataḥ
ekaṃ daśa ca vastrāṇiṃ teṣāmagre prakīrya ca
teṣu vastreṣu niḥkṣipyatilādyāni pṛthakpṛthak
kāṃsyapātraṃ śatapalaṃ vibhidyaikādaśāṃśakam
ikṣudaṇḍaṃ ca dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ
gośṛge tu hiraṇyena dvinīṣkeṇa tu kārayet
padmasya pūrvadigbhāge viprāndvādaśa pūjitān
etenaiva tu mārgeṇa teṣu śraddhāsamanvitaḥ
pūrvavaddakṣiṇe bhāge viprānṣoḍaśa saṃsthitān
kevalaṃ rudradānaṃ vā adityebhyo 'tha vā punaḥ
mūrtyādīnāṃ ca vā deyaṃ yathāvibhavavistaram
padmaṃ vinyasya rājāsau śeṣaṃ vā kārayennṛpaḥ
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā pañcaniṣkeṇa bhūṣaṇam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tiladhenudānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
gosahasrapradānaṃ ca vadāmi śṛṇu suvrata
gavāṃ sahasramādāya savatsaṃ saguṇaṃ śubham
tāsāṃ śṛṅgāṇi hemnātha pratiniṣkeṇa bandhayet
śivāya dadyādviprebhyo dakṣiṇāṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak
daśaniṣkaṃ tadardhaṃ vā tasyārdhārdhamathāpi vā
yathāvibhavavistāraṃ niṣkamātramathāpi vā
gāvaścārādhya yatnena dātavyāḥ sumanoramāḥ
gāvo mamāgrato nityaṃ gāvo naḥ pṛṣṭhatastathā
hṛdaye me sadā gāvo gāvaṃ madhye vasāmy aham
iti kṛtvā dvijāgryebhyodattvā gatvā pradakṣiṇam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge gosahasrapradānaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
hiraṇyāśvapradānaṃ ca vadāmī vijayāvaham
aśvamedhātpunaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ vadāmī śṛṇu suvrata
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa aṣṭottaraśatena vā
kṛtvāśvaṃ lakṣaṇairyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam
pañcakalyāṇasaṃpannaṃ divyākāraṃ tu kārayet
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvāṅgaiśca samanvitam
tanmadhyadeśe saṃsthāpya turaṅgaṃ svaguṇānvitam
tasya pūrvādiśābhāge brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam
suredrabuddhyā saṃpūjya pañcaniṣkaṃ pradāpayet
sa cāśvaḥ śivabhaktāya dātavyo vidhinaiva tu
suvarṇāśvaṃ pradattvā tu ācāryamapi pūjayet
yathāvibhavavistāraṃ pañcaniṣkamathāpivā
dīnāndhakṛpaṇānāthabālavṛddhakṛśāturān
toṣayedannadānena brāhmaṇāṃśca viśeṣataḥ
etadyaḥ kurute bhaktyā dānamaśvasya mānavaḥ
eendrānbhogāṃściraṃ bhuktvā ruciraiśvaryavānbhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hiraṇyāśvadānaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
kanyāṃ lakṣaṇasaṃpannāṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitām
mātāpitrostu saṃvādaṃ kṛtvā dattvā dhanaṃ mahat
ātmīkṛtyātha saṃsnāpya vastraṃ dattvā śubhaṃ navam
bhūṣaṇairbhūṣayitvātha gandhamālyairathārcayet
nimittāni samīkṣyātha gotranakṣatrakādikān
dātavyā śrotriyāyaiva brāhmaṇāya tapasvine
sākṣādadhītavedāya vidhinā brahmacāriṇe
dāsadāsīdhanāḍhyaṃ ca bhūṣaṇāniṃ viśeṣataḥ
kṣetrāṇi ca dhanaṃ dhānya vāsāṃsi ca pradāpayet
yāvanti dehe romāṇi kanyāyāḥ saṃtatau punaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kanyādānavidhirnāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
hiraṇyavṛṣadānaṃ ca kathayāmi samāsataḥ
vṛṣarūpaṃ hiraṇyena sahasreṇātha kārayet
tadardhārdhena vā dhīmāṃstadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
aṣṭottaraśatenāpi vṛṣabhaṃ dharmarūpiṇam
lalāṭe kārayetpuṇḍramardhacandrakalākṛtim
grīvāyāṃ ghāṇṭavalayaṃ ratnacitraṃ tu kārayet
vṛṣāṅkaṃ kārayettatra kiṅkiṇīvalayāvṛtam
vṛṣendraṃ sthāpayettatra paścimāmukhamagrataḥ
īśvaraṃ pūjayedbhaktyā vṛṣārūḍhaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
vṛṣendraṃ pūjya gāyatryā namaskṛtya samāhitaḥ
tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāya vidmahe dharmapādāya dhīmahi
tanno vṛṣaḥ pracodayāt
mantreṇānena saṃpūjya vṛṣaṃ dharmavivṛddhaye
vṛṣabhaḥ pūjya dātavyo brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śivāya vā
dakṣiṇā caiva dātavyā yathāvittānusārataḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge suvarṇavṛṣadānaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
gajadānaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
dvijāya vā śivāyātha dātavyaḥ pūjya pūrvavat
gajaṃ sulakṣaṇopetaṃ haimaṃ vā rājataṃ tu vā
tadardhārdhena vā kuryātsarvalakṣaṇabhūṣitam
aṣṭamyāṃ vā pradātavyaṃ śivāya parameṣṭhine
brāhmaṇāya daridrāya śrotriyāyāhitāgnaye
śivamuddiśya dātavyaṃ śivaṃ saṃpūjya pūrvavat
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
lokapālāṣṭakaṃ divyaṃ sākṣātparamadurlabham
svadeśarakṣaṇaṃ divyaṃ gajavājivivardhanam
putra vṛddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ gobrāhmaṇahitāvaham
digvidikṣu prakartavyaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vālukāmayam
aṣṭau viprānsamabhyarcya vedavedāṅgapāragān
jitendriyānkulodbhūtānsarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutān
śivābhimukhamāsīnānāhateṣvaṃbareṣu ca
gandhapuṣpaiḥ sudhūpaiśca brāhmaṇānarcayetkramāt
samiddhṛtābhyāṃ hotavyamagnikāryaṃ krameṇa vā
evaṃ hutvā vidhānena ācāryaḥ śivavatsalaḥ
yajamānaṃ samāhūya sarvābharamabhūṣitān
pṛthakpṛthaktanmantraiśca daśaniṣkaṃ ca bhūṣaṇam
daśanīṣkeṇa kartavyamāsanaṃ kevalaṃ pṛthak
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā yathāvibhavavistaram
evaṃ yaḥ kurute dānaṃ lokeśānāṃ tu bhaktitaḥ
lokeśānāṃ ciraṃ sthitvā sārvabhaumau bhavedbudhaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
pūrvoktadeśakāle ca maṇḍape ca vidhānataḥ
praṇayātkuṇḍamadhye ca sthaṇḍile śivasannidhau
pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ samāsādya padmayonimataḥ param
mantrābhyāṃ vidhinoktābhyāṃ praṇavādisamantrakam
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt
śivāya haraye svāhā svadhā vauṣaṭvaṣaṭ tathā
pūjayitvā vidhānena paścāddhomaṃ samācaret
sarvadravyaṃ hi hotavyaṃ dvābhyāṃ kuṇḍavidhānataḥ
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tebhyaḥ pṛthakpṛthaganuttamam
vastrābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam
gurureko hi vai śrīmān brahmā viṣṇurmaheśvaraḥ
teṣāṃ pṛthakpṛthagdeyaṃ bhojayedbrāhmaṇānapi
śivārcanā ca kartavyā snapanādi yathākramam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
evaṃ ṣoḍaśa dānāni kathitāni śubhāni ca
sūta uvāca
jīvacchrāddhavidhiṃ vakṣye samāsātsarvasaṃmatam
vasiṣṭhāsa ca śiṣṭāya bhṛgave bhārgavāya ca
śrāddhamārgakramaṃ sākṣācchrāddhārhāṇāmapi kramam
viśeṣamapi vakṣyāmi jīvacchrāddhasya suvratāḥ
parvate vā nadītīre vane vāyatane 'pi vā
jīvacchrāddhaṃ prakartavyaṃ mṛtakāle prayatnataḥ
karma kurvannakurvanvā jñānī vājñānavānapi
śrotriyo 'śrotriyo vāpi brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo 'pi vā
vaiśyo vā nātra saṃdeho yogamārgagato yatā
parīkṣya bhūmiṃ vidhivadgandhavarṇarasādibhiḥ
śalyamuddhṛtya yatnena sthāṇḍilaṃ saikataṃ bhuvi
madhyato hastamātreṇa kuṇḍaṃ caivāyataṃ śubham
sthāṇḍilaṃ vā prakartavyamiṣumātraṃ punaḥ punaḥ
anvādhāya yathāśāstraṃ parigṛhya ca sarvataḥ
paristīrya svaśākhoktaṃ pāraṃparyakramāgatam
ādau kṛtvā samiddhomaṃ caruṇā ca pṛthakpṛthak
oṃ bhūḥ brahmaṇe namaḥ
oṃ bhūḥ brahmaṇe svāhā
oṃ bhuvaḥ viṣṇave namaḥ
oṃ bhuvaḥ viṣṇave svāhā
oṃ svaḥ rudrāya namaḥ
oṃ svaḥ rudrāya svāhā
oṃ mahaḥ īśvarāya namaḥ
oṃ mahaḥ īśvarāya svāhā
oṃ janaḥ prakṛtaye namaḥ
oṃ janaḥ prakṛtaye svāhā
oṃ tapaḥ mudgalāya namaḥ
oṃ tapaḥ mudgalāya svāhā
oṃ ṛtaṃ puruṣāya namaḥ
oṃ ṛtaṃ paruṣāya svāhā
oṃ satyaṃ śivāya namaḥ
oṃ satyaṃ śivāya svāhā
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvāya devāya bhūrnamaḥ
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvāya bhūḥ svāhā
śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvasya devasya patnyai bhūrnamaḥ
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ sarvapatnyaibhūḥ svāhā
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyaṃ rasaṃ bhavāya devāya bhuvo namaḥ
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavāya devāya bhuvaḥ svāhā
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavasya patnyai bhuvaḥ svāhā
rudrāgniṃ me gopāya netre rūpaṃ rudrāya devāya svarāeṃ namaḥ
rudrāgniṃ me gopāya netre rūpaṃ rudrāya devāya svaḥ svāhā
rudrāgniṃ me gāpāya netre rūpaṃ rudrasya patnyai svarāeṃ namaḥ
ugra vāyuṃ me gopāya tvaci sparśaṃ ugrāya devāya maharnamaḥ
ugra vāyūṃ me gopāya tvaci sparśamugrāya devāya mahaḥ svāhā
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmāya devāya jano namaḥ
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmāya devāya janaḥ svāhā
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmasya patnyai jano namaḥ
bhīma suṣiraṃ me gopāya śrotre śabdaṃ bhīmasya devasya patnyai janaḥ svāhā
īśa rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇāmīśāya devāya tapo namaḥ
īśa rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇamīśāya devāya tapaḥ svāhā
rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇāmīśasya patnyai tapo namaḥ
īśa rajo me gopāya dravye tṛṣṇamīśasya patnyai tapaḥ svāhā
mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ dharme mahādevāya ṛtaṃ namaḥ
mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ dharme mahādevāya ṛtaṃ svāhā
mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ dharme mahādevāya patnyai ṛtaṃ namaḥ
mahādeva satyaṃ ma gopāya śraddhāṃ mahādevasya patnyai ṛtaṃ svāhā
paśupate pāśaṃ me gopāya bhoktṛtvabhogyaṃ paśupataye devāya satyaṃ namaḥ
paśupate pāśaṃ me gopāya bhoktṛtvabhāgyaṃ paśupataye devasya satyaṃ svāhā
oṃ paśupate pāśaṃ me gopāya yoktṛtvabhogyaṃ paśupater devasya patnyai satyaṃ namaḥ
oṃ paśupate pāśaṃ ma gopāya yoktṛtvabhogyaṃ paśupaterdevasya patnyai satyaṃ svāhā
oṃ śivāya namaḥ
oṃ śivāya satyaṃ svāhā
evaṃ śivāya hotavyaṃ viriñcyādyaṃ ca pūvavat
viriñcādyaṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ sṛṣṭimārgeṣu suvratāḥ
punaḥ paśupateḥ patnīṃ tathā paśupatīṃ kramāt
carvantamājyapūrvaṃ ca samidantaṃ samāhitaḥ
oṃ śarva dharāṃ me chindhi ghrāṇe gandhaṃ chindhi meghaṃ jahi bhūḥ svāhā
bhuvaḥ svāhā
svaḥ svāhā
bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā
evaṃ pṛthakpṛthagghutvā kevalena ghṛtena vā
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
virajā ca ghṛtenaiva śatamaṣṭottaraṃ pṛthak
prāṇādibhiśca juhuyāddhṛtenaiva tu kevalam
oṃ prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo ma viśāpradāhāya prāṇāya svāhā
prāṇādhipataye rudrāya vṛṣāntakāya svāhā
oṃ bhūḥ svāhā
oṃ bhuvaḥ svāhā
oṃ svaḥ svāhā
bhūrbhūvaḥ svaḥ svāhā
śarvādīnāṃ ca viprāṇāṃ vastrābharaṇakaṃbalān
vāhanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ kāṃsyatāmrādibhājanam
haimaṃ ca rājataṃ dhenuṃ tilān kṣetraṃ ca vaibhavam
dāsīdāsagaṇaścaiva dātavyo dakṣiṇāmapi
piṇḍaṃ ca pūrvavaddadyātpṛthagaṣṭaprakārataḥ
brāhmaṇānaṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayecca sadakṣiṇam
viśeṣa evaṃ kathita aśeṣaśrāddhacoditaḥ
bāndhave 'pi mṛte tasya śaucāśaucaṃ na vidyate
sūtakaṃ ca na saṃdehaḥ snānamātreṇa śuddhyati
paścājjāte kumāre ca sve kṣetre cātmano yadi
kanyakā yadi rāñjātā paścāttasya mahātmanaḥ
ekaparṇā iva jñeyā aparṇā iva suvratā
mucyante karmaṇānena mātṛtaḥ pitṛtastathā
putrakṛtyamaśeṣaṃ ca kṛtvā doṣo na vidyate
brahmaṇākathitaṃ sarvaṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām
punaḥ sanatkumārāya kathitaṃ tena dhīmatā
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāyaiva kathitaṃ brahmasūnunā
jñātaṃ mayā kṛtaṃ caiva niyogādeva tasya tu
muniputrāya dātavyaṃ na cābhaktāya suvratāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge jīvacchrādvavidhirnāma pañcacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
mṛrkhāṇāmapi mokṣārthamasmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa
rudrādityavasūnāṃ ca śakraādīnāṃ ca suvrata
pratiṣṭhā kīdṛśī śaṃbhorligamūrteśca śobhanā
viṣṇoḥ śakrasya devasya brahmaṇaśca mahātmanaḥ
vāyoḥ somasya yakṣasya kuberasyāmitātmanaḥ
īśānasya dharāyāśca śrīpratiṣṭhātha vā katham
durgāśivāpratiṣṭhā ca haimavatyāśca śobhanā
skandasya gaṇarājasya nandinaśca viśeṣataḥ
tathānyeṣāṃ ca devānāṃ gaṇānāmapi vā punaḥ
pratiṣṭhālakṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ vistāradvaktumarhasi
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasyāsi sākṣāttvamaparā tanuḥ
iti vyāsasya vipulā gāthā bhāgīrathītaṭe
ekaḥ samo vā bhinno vā śiṣyastasya mahādyuteḥ
vaiśaṃpāyanatulyo 'si vyāsaśiṣyeṣu bhūtale
babhūva vismayo 'tīva munīnāṃ tasya cāgrataḥ
athāntarikṣe vipulā sākṣāddevī sarasvatī
alaṃ munīnāṃ praśro 'yamiti vācā babhūva ha
sarvaṃ liṅgamayaṃ lokaṃ sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam
liṅgasthāpanasanmārganihitasvāyatāsinā
āśu brahmāṇḍamudbhidya nirgacchedaviśaṅkayā
upedrāṃbhojagarbhendrayamāṃbudhanadeśvarāḥ
tathānye ca śivaṃ sthāpya liṅgamūrti maheśvaram
sveṣusveṣu ca pakṣeṣu pradhānāste yathā dvijāḥ
brahmā haraśca bhagavānviṣṇurdevī ramā dharā
lakṣmīrdhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ prajñā dharā durgā śacī tathā
rudrāśca vasavaḥ skando viśākhaḥ śākha eva ca
naigameśaśca bhagavāṃllokapālā grahāstathā
sarve nandipurogāśca gaṇā gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ
pitaro munayaḥ sarve kuberādyāśca suprabhāḥ
āditya vasavaḥ sāṃkhyā aśvinau ca bhiṣagvarau
viśvedevāśca sādhyāśca paśavaḥ pakṣiṇo mṛgāḥ
brahmādisthāvarāntaṃ ca sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam
yatnena stāpitaṃ sarvaṃ pūjitaṃ pūjayedyadi
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
iti niśamya kṛtāñjalaya stadā divi mahāmunayaḥ kṛtaniścayāḥ
śivataraṃ śivamīśvaramavyayaṃ manasi liṅgamayaṃ praṇipatya te
munivarāśca gaṇāśca surāsurā naravarāḥ śivaliṅgamayāḥ punaḥ
śrutvaivaṃ munayaḥ sarve ṣaṭkulīyāḥ samāhitāḥ
saṃtyajya sarvaṃ devasya pratiṣṭhāṃ kartumudyatāḥ
apṛcchansūtamanaghaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā
liṅgapratiṣṭhāṃ vipulāṃ sarve te śaṃsitavratāḥ
sūta uvāca
pratiṣṭhāṃ liṅgamūrtervo yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
kṛtvaiva liṅgaṃ vidhinā bhuvi liṅgeṣu yatnataḥ
liṅgamekatamaṃ śailaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam
hemaratnamayaṃ vāpi rājataṃ tāmrajaṃ tu vā
liṅgavedī umā devī liṅgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ
tayoḥ sapūjanādeva devī devaśca pūjitau
pratiṣṭhayā ca deveśo devyā sārdhaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
tasmātsavedikaṃ liṅgaṃ sthāpayetsthāpakottamaḥ
mūle brahmā vasati bhagavānmadhyabhāge ca viṣṇuḥ sarveśānaḥ
pūjayecca viśeṣeṇa liṅgaṃ sarvārthasiddhaye
kūrcavastrādibhirliṅgamācchādya kalaśaiḥ punaḥ
lokapālādidaivatyaiḥ sakūrcaiḥ sākṣataiḥ śubhaiḥ
utkūrcaiḥ svastikādyaiśca citratantukaveṣṭitaiḥ
lakṣayetparito liṅgamīśānena pratiṣṭhitam
dhūpadīpasamopetaṃ vitānavitatāṃbaram
lokapāladhvajaiścaiva gajādimahiṣādibhiḥ
citritaiḥ pūjitaiścaiva darbhamālā ca śobhanā
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā tayā bāhye ca veṣṭayet
pañcāhaṃ vā tryahaṃvātha ekarātramadhāpi vā
vedādhyayanasaṃpanno nṛtyagītādimaṅgalaiḥ
kiṅkiṇīravakopetaṃ tālavīṇāravairapi
īkṣayetkālamavyagro yajamānaḥ samāhitaḥ
utthāpya svastikaṃ dhyāyenmaṇḍape lakṣaṇānvite
saṃskṛte vedisaṃyukte navakuṇḍena saṃvṛte
aṣṭamaṇḍalasaṃyukte digdhvajāṣṭakasaṃyute
pūrvoktalakṣaṇopetaiḥ kuṇḍaiḥ prāgāditaḥ kramāt
pradhānaṃ kuṇḍamīśānyāṃ caturasraṃ vidhīyate
athavā pañcakuṇḍaikaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ caikameva ca
yajñopakaraṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ śivārcāyāṃ hi bhūṣaṇaiḥ
vedimadhye mahāśayyāṃ pañcatūlīprakalpitām
kalpayetkāñcanopetāṃ sitavastrāvaguṇṭhitām
prākśiraskaṃ nyaselliṅgamīśānena yathāvidhi
ratnanyāse kṛte pūrva kevalaṃ kalaśaṃ nyaset
liṅgamācchādya vastrābhyāṃ kūrcena ca samantataḥ
ratnanyāse prasakte 'tha vāmādyā nava śaktayaḥ
navaratnaṃ hiraṇyādyaiḥ pañcagavyena saṃyutaiḥ
viṣṇugāyatriyā bhāgaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tvatha vinyaset
sarvaṃ namaḥ śivāyeti namo haṃsaḥ śivāya ca
madhyakuṃbhe śivaṃ devīṃ dakṣiṇe parameśvarīm
brahmāṇaṃ skandakuṃbhe vā īśakumbhe hariṃ tathā
athavā śivakuṃbhe ca brahmāṅgāni ca vinyaset
śivo maheśvaraścaiva rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ
brahmāṇyevaṃ samāsena hṛdayādīni cāṃbikā
vardhanyāmāpi yatnena gāyatryaṅgaiśca suvratāḥ
vidyeśvarāndiśaṃ kuṃbhe brahmakūrcena pūrite
aṃnateśādidevāṃśca praṇavādinamontakam
navavastraṃ pratighaṭamaṣṭakuṃbheṣu dāpayet
vidyeśvarāṇāṃ kuṃbheṣu hemaratnādi vinyaset
jayādisviṣṭaparyantaṃ sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret
paitā mahena kuṃbhena brahmabhāgaṃ viśeṣataḥ
vidyeśvarāṇāṃ kuṃbhaiśca secayetparameśvaram
pūjayetsnapanaṃ kṛtvā sahasrādiṣu saṃbhavaiḥ
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā sahasrapaṇamuttamam
itareṣāṃ tadardhaṃ syāttadardhaṃ vā vidhīyate
vastrāṇi ca pradhānasya kṣetrabhūṣaṇagodhanam
navāhaṃ vāpi saptāhamekāhaṃ ca tryahaṃ tathā
devānāṃ bhāskarādīnāṃ homaṃ pūrvavadeva tu
ya evaṃ sthāpayelliṅgaṃ sa eva parameśvaraḥ
tena devagaṇā rudrā ṛṣayo 'psarasastathā
sthāpitāḥ pūjitāścaiva trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge liṅgasthāpanaṃ nāma saptacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
sarveṣāmapi devānāṃ pratiṣṭhāmapi vistarāt
sthāpayedutsavaṃ kṛtvā pūjayecca vidhānataḥ
bhānoḥ pañcāgninā kāryaṃ dvādaśāgnikrameṇa vā
sarvakuṇḍāni vṛttāni padmākārāṇi suvratāḥ
aṃbāyā yonikuṇḍaṃ syādvardhanyekā vidhīyate
śaktīnāṃ sarvakāryeṣu yonikuṇḍaṃ vidhīyate
gāyatrīṃ kalpayecchaṃbhoḥ sarveṣāmapi yatnataḥ
sarve rudrāṃśajā yasmātsaṃkṣepeṇa vadāmi vaḥ
gāyatrībhedāḥ
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi
tannaḥ śivaḥ pracodayāt
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe vakratuṇḍāya dhīmahi
mahāsenāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi
tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāya vidmahe vedapādāya dhīmahi
tanno vṛṣaḥ pracodayāt
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt
tanno lakṣmīḥ pracodayāt
tannaḥ sraṣṭā pracodayāt
śivāsyajāyai vidmahe devarūpāyai dhīmahi
tanno vācā pracodayāt
tannaḥ śakraḥ pracodayāt
niśācarāya vidmahe khaḍgahastāya dhīmahi
śuddhahastāya vidmahe pāśahastāya dhīmahi
sarpaprāṇāya vidmahe yaṣṭihastāya dhīmahi
yakṣeśvarāya vidmahe gadāhastāya dhīmahi
sarveśvarāya vidmahe śūlahastāya dhīmahi
evaṃ prabhidya gāyatrīṃ tattadevānurūpataḥ
pūjayet sthāpayetteṣāmāsanaṃ praṇavaṃ smṛtam
athavā viṣṇumatulaṃ sūktena puruṣeṇa vā
viṣṇuṃ caiva mahāviṣṇuṃ sadāviṣṇumanukramāt
vāsudevaḥ pradhānastu tataḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ svayam
bahūni vividhānīha tasya śāpodbhavāni ca
sarvāvarteṣu rūpāṇi jagatāṃ ca hitāya vai
matsyaḥ kūrmo 'tha vārāho nārasiṃho 'tha vāmanaḥ
rāmo rāmaśca kṛṣṇaśca bauddhaḥ kalkī tathaiva ca
teṣāmapi ca gāyatrīṃ kṛtvā stāpya ca pūjayet
vijñānāni ca yantrāṇi mantropaniṣadāni ca
pañca brahmāṅgajānīha pañcabhūtamayāni ca
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ paramaśobhanaḥ
hareraṣṭākṣarāṇīha praṇavena samāsataḥ
oṃ namo vāsudevāya namaḥ saṃkarṣaṇāya ca
biṃbāniyāni devasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
pratiṣṭhā caiva pūjā ca liṅgavanmunisattamāḥ
kṣetrapradakṣiṇaṃ caiva ārāmasya purasya ca
kuṇḍamaṇḍapanirmāṇaṃ śayanaṃ ca vidhīyate
hutvā navāgnibhāgena navakuṇḍe yatāvidhi
athavā pañcakuṇḍeṣu pradhāne kevale 'tha vā
pratiṣṭhā kathitā divyā pāraṃparyakramāgatā
śilodbhavānāṃ biṃbānāṃ citrābhāsasya vā punaḥ
jalādhivāsanaṃ proktaṃ vṛṣendrasya prakīrtitam
prāsādasya pratiṣṭhāyāṃ pratiṣṭhā parikīrtitā
prāsādāṅgasya sarvasya yathāṅgānāṃ tanoriva
vṛṣāgnimātṛvighneśakumārānapi yatnataḥ
śreṣṭhāṃ durgāṃ tathā caṇḍīṃ gāyatryā vai yathāvidhi
prāgādyaṃ sthāpayecchaṃbhoraṣṭāvaraṇamuttamam
lokapālagaṇeśādyānapi śaṃbhoḥ pravinyaset
umā caṇḍī ca nandī ca mahākālo mahāmuniḥ
vighneśvaro mahābhṛṅgī skandaḥ saumyāditaḥ kramāt
indrādīnsveṣu sthāneṣu brahmāṇaṃ ca janārdanam
siṃhāsane hyanantādīn vidyeśāmapi ca kramāt
sthāpayetpraṇavenaiva guhyāṅgādīni paṅkaje
sarveṣāmapi devānāṃ devīnāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge 'ṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
aghoreśasya mahātmyaṃ bhavatā kathitaṃ purā
pūjāṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ devasya bhagavanvaktumarhasi
sūta uvāca
aghoreṇāṅga yuktena vidhivacca viśeṣataḥ
pratiṣṭhāliṅgavidhinā nānyatā munipuṅgavāḥ
tathāgnipūjāṃ vai kuryādyathā pūjā tathaiva ca
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
vyādhīnāṃ nāśanaṃ caiva tilahomastu bhūtidaḥ
sahasreṇa mahābhūtiḥ śatena vyādhināśanam
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa ṣaṇmāsājjāyate dhruvam
siddhayo naiva saṃdeho rājyamaṇḍālināmapi
trikālaṃ māsamekaṃ tu sahasraṃ juhuyātpayaḥ
yavakṣīrājyahomena jātitaṇḍulakena vā
prīyeta bhagavānīśo hyaghoraḥ parameśvaraḥ
dadhnā puṣṭirnṛpāṇāṃ ca kṣīrahomena śāntikam
ṣaṇmāsaṃ tu ghṛtaṃ hutvā sarvavyādhivināśanam
rājayakṣmā tilairhemānnaśyate vatsareṇa tu
sarvakuṣṭhakṣayārthaṃ ca madhunāktaiśca taṇḍulaiḥ
juhuyādayutaṃ nityaṃ ṣaṇmāsānniyataḥ sadā
kevalaṃ ghṛtahomena sarvarogakṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ
sarvavyādhi haraṃ dhyānaṃ sthāpanaṃ vidhinārcanam
pratiṣṭhā yajanaṃ sarvaṃ nandinā kathitaṃ purā
brahmaputrāya śiṣyāya tena vyāsāya suvratāḥ
śrīlīṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekonapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nigrahaḥ kathitastena śivavaktreṇa śūlinā
kṛtāparāndhināṃ taṃ tu vaktumarhasi suvrata
tvayā navidinaṃ nāsti laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ tathā
śrautaṃ smārtaṃ mahābhāga romaharṣaṇa suvrata
sūta uvāca
purā bhṛgusutenokto hiraṇyākṣāya suvratāḥ
nigraho 'ghoraśiṣyeṇa śukreṇākṣayatejasā
tasya prasādaddaityendro hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān
utpādya putraṃ gaṇapaṃ cāndhakaṃ cāruvikramam
rarāja loke devena varāheṇa niṣūditaḥ
strībādhāṃ bālabādhāṃ ca gavāmapi viśeṣataḥ
tena daityena sā devī dharā nītā rasātalam
tenāghoreṇa devena niṣphalo nigrahaḥ kṛtaḥ
saṃvatsara sahasrānte varāheṇa ca sūditaḥ
strīṇāmapi viśeṣeṇa gavāmapi na kārayet
ātatāyinamuddiśya kartavyaṃ nṛpasattamaiḥ
brāhmaṇebhyo na kartavyaṃ svarāṣṭreśasya vā punaḥ
kṛtamātre na saṃdeho nigrahaḥ saṃprajāyate
lakṣamātraṃ pumāñjaptvā aghoraṃ ghorarūpiṇam
daśāṃśaṃ vidhinā hutvā tilena dvijasattamāḥ
saṃpūjya lakṣapuṣpeṇa sitena vidhipūrvakam
bāṇaliṅge 'thavā vahnau dakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
siddhamantro 'nyatā nāsti draṣṭā siddhyādayaḥ punaḥ
siddhamantraḥ svayaṃ kuryātpretasthāne viśeṣataḥ
mātṛsthāne 'pi vā vidvānvedavedāṅgapāragaḥ
kevalaṃ mantrasiddho vā brāhmaṇaḥ śivabhāvitaḥ
kuryādvidhimimaṃ dhīmānātmanor'thaṃ nṛpasya vā
sūlāṣṭakaṃ nyasedvidvānpūrvādīśānakāntakam
triśikhaṃ ca triśūlaṃ ca caturviśācchikāgrataḥ
aghoravigrahaṃ kṛtvā saṃkalīkṛtavigrahaḥ
sarvanāśakaraṃ dhyātvā sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
kālāgnikoṭisaṃkāśaṃ svadehamapi bhāvayet
śūlaṃ kapālaṃ pāśaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ caiva śarāsanam
bāṇaṃ ḍamarukaṃ khaḍgamaṣṭāyudhamanukramāt
aṣṭahastaśca varado nīlakaṇṭho digaṃbaraḥ
daṃṣṭrākarālavadano raudradṛṣṭirbhayaṅkaraḥ
huṃphaṭkāramahāśabdaśabditākhiladiṅmukhaḥ
trinetraṃ nāgapāśena subaddhamukuṭaṃ svayam
sarvābharaṇasaṃpannaṃ pretabhasmāvaguṇṭhitam
bhūtaiḥ pretaiḥ piśācaiśca ḍākinībhiśca rākṣasaiḥ
saṃvṛtaṃ gajakṛttvā ca sarpabhūṣaṇabhūṣitam
vṛścikābharaṇaṃ devaṃ nīlanīradanisvanam
nīlāñjanādrisaṃkāśaṃ siṃhacarmottarīyakam
ṣaṭtriṃśaduktamātrābhiḥ prāṇāyāmena suvratāḥ
mahāmudrāsamāyuktaḥ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
kauberyāṃ vidivatkṛtvā homakuṇḍāni śāstrataḥ
ācāryo madhyakuṇḍe tu sādhakāśca diśāsu vai
paristīrya vilomena pūrvavacchūlasaṃbhṛtaḥ
kālāgnipīṭhamadhyasthaḥ svayaṃ śiṣyaiśca tādṛśaiḥ
dhyātvā ghoramaghoreśaṃ dvātriṃśākṣarasaṃyutam
vibhītakena vai kṛtvā dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ
pīṭhe nyasya nṛpendrasya śatrumaṅgārakeṇa tu
kuṇḍasyādhaḥ khanecchatruṃ brāhmaṇaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ
śmaśānāṅgāramānīya tuṣeṇa saha dāhayet
tatrāgniṃ sthāpayettūṣṇīṃ brahmacaryaparāyaṇaḥ
māyūrāstreṇa nābhyāṃ tu jvalanaṃ dīpayettataḥ
kañcukaṃ tuṣasaṃyuktaiḥ kārpāsāsthisamanvitaiḥ
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ tu homayedanupūrvaśaḥ
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ samārabhya yathākramam
aṣṭamyantaṃ tathāṅgāramaṇḍalasthānavarjitaḥ
evaṃ kṛte nṛpendrasya śatravaḥ kulajaiḥ saha
mantreṇānena cādāya nṛkapāle nakhaṃ tathā
keśaṃ nṛṇāṃ tathāṅgāraṃ tuṣaṃ kañcukameva ca
cīracchaṭāṃ rājadhūlīṃ gṛhasaṃmārjanasya vā
viṣasarpasya dantāni vṛṣadantāni yāni tu
tathā kṛṣṇamṛgāṇāṃ ca biḍālasya ca pūrvavat
daṃṣṭrāṇi sādhayitvā tu mantreṇānena suvratāḥ
tatkapālaṃ nakhaṃ kṣetre gṛhe vā nagare 'pi vā
pretasthāne 'pi vā rāṣṭre mṛtavastreṇa veṣṭayet
śatroraṣṭamārāśau vā pariviṣṭe divākare
some vā pariviṣṭe tu mantreṇānena suvratāḥ
sthānanāśo bhavettasya śatrornāśaśca jāyate
śatruṃ rājñaḥ samālikhya gamane samavasthite
catustoraṇasaṃyukte darbhamālāsamāvṛte
vedādhyayanasaṃpanne rāṣṭre vṛddhiprakāśake
dakṣiṇena tu pādena mūrdhni saṃtāḍayetsvayam
evaṃ kṛte nṛpendrasya śatrunāśo bhaviṣyati
svārāṣṭrapatimuddiśya yaḥ kuryādābhicārikam
sa ātmānaṃ nihatyaiva svakulaṃ nāśayetkudhīḥ
tasmātsvarāṣṭragāṃptāraṃ nṛpatiṃ pālayetsadā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
sūta uvāca
vajravāhanikā nāma sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī
anayā secayedvajraṃ nṛpāṇāṃ sādhayettathā
tataścākṣaralakṣaṃ ca japedvidvānsamāhitaḥ
vajrīdaśāṃśaṃ juhuyādvajrakuṇḍe ghṛtādibhiḥ
tena vajreṇa vai gacchañchatrūñjīyādraṇājire
devī śakropakārārthaṃ sākṣādvajreśvarī tathā
purā tvaṣṭa prajānātho hataputraḥ sureśvarāt
tasminyajñe yatāprāptaṃ vidinopakṛtaṃ haviḥ
bhāgaṃ bhāgārhatā naiva viśvarūpo hatastvayā
ityuktvā cāśramaṃ sarvaṃ mohayāmāsa māyayā
tato māyāṃ vinirbhidya viśvarūpavimardanaḥ
tatastaccheṣamādāya krodhāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ
tataḥ kālāgnisaṃkāśo vartanādvṛtrasaṃjñitaḥ
prādurāsīt sureśārir dudrāva ca vṛṣāntakaḥ
tataḥ kirīṭī bhagavānparityajya divaṃ kṣaṇāt
tadā tamāha sa vibhṛrhṛṣṭo brahmā ca viśvasṛṭ
tasmādvajreśvarīvidyā sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī
mandehā rākṣasā nityaṃ vijitā vidyayaiva tu
tāṃ vidyāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapramocanīm
vidyā vajreśvarītyeṣā sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī
anayā saṃhṛtiḥ śaṃbhorvidyāyā munipuṅgavāḥ
iti śrīliṃṅgamahāpārāṇe uttarabhāge ekapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
śrutā vajreśvarī vidyā brāhmī śakropakāriṇī
anayā sarvakāryāṇi nṛpāmāmiti naḥ śrutam
viniyogaṃ vadasvāsyā vidyāyā romaharṣaṇa
sūta uvāca
vaśyamākarṣaṇaṃ caiva vidveṣaṇamataḥ param
uccāṭanaṃ staṃbhanaṃ ca mohanaṃ tāḍanaṃ tathā
utsādanaṃ tathā chedaṃ māraṇaṃ pratibandhanam
senāstaṃbhanakādīni sāvitryā sarvamācaret
udvāsyānena mantreṇa gantavyaṃ nānyathā dvijāḥ
pratikāryaṃ tathā bāhyaṃ kṛtvā paśyādikāṃ kriyām
devīmāvāhya ca punarjapetsaṃpūjayetpunaḥ
sarvakāryāṇi vidhinā sādhayedvidyayā punaḥ
jātīpuṣpaiśca vaśyārthi juhuyādayutatrayam
ghṛtena karavīreṇa kuryādākarṣaṇaṃ dvijāḥ
vidveṣaṇaṃ viśeṣeṇa kuryāllāṅgalakasya ca
tailenoccāṭanaṃ proktaṃ staṃbhanaṃ madhunā smṛtam
tilena mohanaṃ proktaṃ tāḍanaṃ rudhireṇa ca
staṃbhanaṃ sarṣapeṇāpi pāṭanaṃ cākuśena ca
māraṇoccāṭane caiva rohībījena suvratāḥ
kunaṭyā niyataṃ vidyātpūjayetparameśvarīm
jayādiprabhṛtīnsarvān sviṣṭāntaṃ pūrvavatsmṛtam
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ prokto viniyogotivistṛtaḥ
japedvā kevalāṃ vidyāṃ saṃpūjya ca vidhānataḥ
sarvasiddhimavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
mṛtyuñjayavidhiṃ sūta brahmakṣatraviśāmapi
mṛtyuñjayavidhiṃ vakṣye bahunā kiṃ dvijottamāḥ
rudrādhyāyena vidhinā ghṛtena niyutaṃ kramāt
dūrvayā ghṛtagokṣīramiśrayā madhunā tathā
caruṇā saghṛtenaiva kevalaṃ payasāpi vā
juhuyātkāla mṛtyorvā pratīkāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
pūjayedbāṇaliṅge vā svayaṃbhūte 'pi vā punaḥ
āyurvedavidairvāpi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa puṇḍarīkeṇa śaṅkaram
saṃpūjya pāyasaṃ dattvā saghṛtaṃ caudanaṃ punaḥ
mudgānnaṃ madhunā yuktaṃ bhakṣyāṇi surabhīṇi ca
pūrvoktairapi puṣpaiśca caruṇā ca viśeṣataḥ
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayedvai sadakṣiṇam
gavāṃ sahasraṃ dattvā tu hiraṇyamapi dāpayet
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sarahasyaṃ samāsataḥ
śivena devadevena śarveṇātyugraśūlinā
sākṣātsanatkumāreṇa sarvalokahitaiṣiṇā
pārāśaryāya kathitaṃ pāraṃparyakramāgatam
śuke gate parandhāma dṛṣṭvā rudraṃ triyaṃbakam
gataśoko mahābhāgo vyasaḥ para ṛṣiḥ prabhuḥ
triyaṃbakasya māhātmyaṃ mantrasya ca viśeṣataḥ
kathitaṃ bahudhā tasmai kṛṣṇadvaipāyānāya vai
lakṣahomena rājyārthī rājyaṃ labdhvā sukhī bhavet
putrārthī putramāpnoti niyutena na saṃśayaḥ
dhanadhānyādibhiḥ sarvaiḥ saṃpūrṇaḥ sarvamaṅgalaiḥ
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet
trayāṇāmapi lokānāṃ guṇānāmapi yaḥ prabhuḥ
vedānāmapi devānāṃ brahmakṣatraviśāmapi
akārokāramakārāṇāṃ mātrāṇāmapi vācakaḥ
aṃbā umā mahādevo hyaṃbakastu triyaṃbakaḥ
supuṣpitasya vṛkṣasya yathā gandhaḥ suśobhanaḥ
vāti dvarāttathā tasya gandhaḥ śaṃbhormahātmanaḥ
gāndhāraścamahādevo devānāmapi līlayā
tasya vīryādabhūdaṇḍaṃ hiraṇmayam ajodbhavam
pañcabhūtānyahaṅkāro buddhiḥ prakṛtireva ca
puṣṭirbījasya tasyaiva tasmādvai puṣṭivardhanaḥ
taṃ puṣṭivardhanaṃ devaṃ ghṛtena payasā tathā
kumudārkaśamīpatragaurasarṣapaśālibhiḥ
hutvā liṅge yathānyāyaṃ bhaktyā devaṃ yajāmahe
ṛtenānena māṃ pāśādbandhanātkarmayogataḥ
mṛtyośca bandanāccaiva mukṣīya bhava tejasā
urvārukāṇāṃ pakvānāṃ yathā kālādabhūtpunaḥ
tathaiva kālaḥ saṃprāpto manunā tena yatnataḥ
evaṃ mantravidhiṃ jñātvā śivaliṅgaṃ samarcayet
tasya pāśakṣayo 'tīva yogino mṛtyunigrahaḥ
triyaṃbakasamo nāsti devo vā ghṛṇayānvitaḥ
prasādaśīlaḥ prītaśca tathā mantropi suvratāḥ
triyaṃbakeṇa mantreṇa pūjayetsusamāhitaḥ
sarvāvasthāṃ gato vāpi mukto 'yaṃ sarvapātakaiḥ
hatvā bhittvā ca bhūtāni bhuktvā cānyāyato 'pi vā
śivamekaṃ sakṛtsmṛtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge cutaṣpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
pūrvamevāpi nikhilaṃ śrutaṃ śrutisamaṃ punaḥ
sūta uvāca
merupṛṣṭhe purā pṛṣṭo munisaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
mithaḥ provāca bhagavānpraṇatāya samāhitaḥ
evaṃ purā mahādevo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
giriputryāṃbayā devyā bhagavatyaikaśayyayā
pṛṣṭaḥ kailāsaśikhare hṛṣṭapuṣṭatanūruhaḥ
śrīdevyuvāca
jñānaṃ ca mokṣadaṃ divyaṃ mucyante yena jantavaḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
bhāvayogastṛtīyaḥ syād abhāvaśca caturthakaḥ
sarvottamo mahāyogaḥ pañcamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
nāḍīśuddhyadhiko yastu recakādikramānvitaḥ
balasthirakriyāyukto dhāraṇādyaiśca śobhanaiḥ
dhāraṇātrayasaṃdīpto bhedatrayaviśodhakaḥ
kuṃbhakāvasthito 'bhyāsaḥ sparśayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
bhāvayogaḥ samākhyātāścittaśuddhipradāyakaḥ
śūnyaṃ sarvaṃ nirābhāsaṃ svarūpaṃ yatra cintyate
abhāvayogaḥ saṃproktaścittanirvāṇakārakaḥ
nīrūpaḥ kevalaḥ śuddhaḥ svacchandaṃ ca suśobhanaḥ
anirdeśyaḥ sadālokaḥ svayaṃvedyaḥ samaṃ tataḥ
svabhāvo bhāsate yatra mahāyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
nirmalaḥ kevalo hyātmā mahāyoga iti smṛtaḥ
aṇimādipradāḥ sarve sarve jñānasya dāyakāḥ
uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyameṣu yogeṣvanukramāt
ahaṃ saṃgavinirmukto mahākāśopamaḥ paraḥ
pravilīno mahānsamyak svayaṃvedyaḥ svasākṣikaḥ
cakāstyānandavapuṣā tena jñeyam idaṃ matam
parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya brāhmaṇāyāhitāgnaye
dhārmikāyākṛtaghnāya dātavyaṃ kramapūrvakam
sādhako jñānasaṃyuktaḥ śrautasmārtaviśāradaḥ
gurubhaktaśca puṇyātmā yogyo yogarataḥ sadā
eva devi samākhyāto yogamārgaḥ sanātanaḥ
pītvā yogāmṛtaṃ yogī mucyate brahmavittamaḥ
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ yogaiśvaryamanuttamam
tasmādiṣṭaiḥ samācāraiḥ śivārcanarataiḥ priye
ityuktvā bhagavāndevīmanujñāpya vṛṣadhvajaḥ
śaṅkukarṇaṃ samāsādya yuyojātmānamātmani
śailādiruvāca
svaṃyabhuva parā mūrtirnūnaṃ brahmamayī varā
bhasmasnāyī bhavennityaṃ yoge pāśupate rataḥ
dhyeyā yathākrameṇaiva vaiṣṇavī ca tataḥ parā
māheśvarī parā paścātsaiva dhyeyā yathākramam
yogeśvarasya yā niṣṭhā saiṣā saṃhṛtya varṇitā
sūta uvāca
evaṃ śilādaputreṇa nandinā kulanandinā
yogaḥ pāśupataḥ prokto bhasmaniṣṭhena dhīmatā
tasmādahamapi śrutvā niyogātsatriṇāmapi
namaḥ śivāya śāntāya vyāsāya munaye namaḥ
granthaikādaśasāhasraṃ purāṇaṃ laiṅgamuttamam
aṣṭottarasatādhyāya mādimāṃśamataḥ param
ṣaṭcatvārīṃśadadhyāyaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam
atha te munayaḥ sarve naimiṣeyāḥ samāhitāḥ
praṇemurdevamīśānaṃ prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ
śākhāṃ paurāṇikīmevaṃ kṛtvaikādaśikāṃ prabhuḥ
laiṅgamādyantamakhilaṃ yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādapi
dvijebhyaḥ śrāvayedvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
yā gatistasya vipulā śāstravidyā ca vaidikī
karmaṇā cāpi miśreṇa kevalaṃ vidyayāpi vā
nivṛttiścāsya viprasya bhavedbhaktiśca śāśvatī
mayi nārāyaṇe deve śraddhā cāstu mahātmanaḥ
vaṃśasya cākṣayā vidyā cāpramādaśca sarvataḥ
ityājñā brahmaṇastasmāttasya sarvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
ṛṣayaḥ procuḥ
ṛṣeḥ sūtasya cāsmākameteṣābhapi cāsya ca
prītiśca vipulā yasmā dasmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa
sā sadāstu virūpākṣaprasādāttu samantataḥ
karābhyāṃ suśubhāgrābhyāṃ sūtaṃ pasparśivāṃstvaci
śraddhā tavāstu cāsmākaṃ namastasmai śivāya ca
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcapañcāśattamodhyāyaḥ
śrībhavānīśaṅkarārpaṇamastu
